	ARG_state_info_setup = yes
	ARG_test_setup_seats = yes
	ARG_setup_positions = yes
	ARG_POL_glow_effect_setup = yes
	ARG_POL_GUI_starting_state_legislature = yes

	ARG_POL_GUI_display_starting_results = yes
	ARG_POL_setup_deps_national_animation = yes
	ARG_POL_sortout_congress = yes
	ARG_POL_sortout_seats_map = yes

	ARG_POL_GUI_set_all_seat_subparty = yes

	}
}

ARG_state_info_setup = {
	#Political Party Number Corresponding
	#0 - PS
	#1 - UCRP
	#2 - UCRI
	#3 - PDC
	#4 - FNPC
	#5 - NP
	#6 - PDP
	#7 - Peronists
	#8 - Other
	#Cycle 1 Senator - Elected Every 3 Years
	#Cycle 2 Senator - Elected Every 6 Years
	#Cycle 3 Senator - Elected Every 9 Years
	#Cycle 1 Deputy - Elected Every 4 Years
	#Cycle 2 Deputy - Elected Every 4 Years
	for_each_loop = {
		array = ARG.ARG_POL_active_parties
		index = idx
		value = party_idx

		set_variable = {target_state = party_idx}
		clear_array = target_state:ARG_senator_locations
	}
	278 = { #Buenos Aires
		set_state_flag = ARG_election_state

		set_variable = {ARG_no_of_cycle_2_deputies = 25}
		set_variable = {ARG_senator_1 = 3}
		set_variable = {ARG_senator_2 = 3}

			ARG_senate_add_to_locations_array = yes
		}

		set_variable = {ARG_POL_party_no = 7}
	}
	8 = {
		clear_array = ARG_POL_coalition_members
		add_to_array = {ARG_POL_coalition_members = 51}
		add_to_array = {ARG_POL_coalition_members = 52}
		add_to_array = {ARG_POL_coalition_members = 53}
		add_to_array = {ARG_POL_coalition_members = 54}

		add_to_array = {ARG_POL_coalition_members = 58}

	}
	ARG_POL_update_active_parties = yes
}
ARG_POL_update_active_parties = {
	clear_array = ARG_POL_active_parties
	clear_array = ARG_POL_active_subparties
	clear_array = ARG_POL_subparties_affiliation
	clear_variable = ARG_POL_number_of_active_parties
	clear_variable = ARG_POL_number_of_active_sub_parties
	for_loop_effect = {
		start = 1
		end = 10
		value = idx

		set_variable = {ARG_party_state = idx}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {ARG_party_state:ARG_POL_coalition_size > 0}
			}
			add_to_array = {ARG_POL_active_parties = ARG_party_state}
			add_to_variable = {ARG_POL_number_of_active_parties = 1}
			add_to_variable = {ARG_POL_number_of_active_sub_parties = ARG_party_state:ARG_POL_coalition_size}
		}
	}
	for_each_scope_loop = {
		array = ARG_POL_active_parties

		for_each_loop = {
			array = ARG_POL_coalition_members
			index = idx

			add_to_array = {ARG.ARG_POL_active_subparties = ARG_POL_coalition_members^idx}
			add_to_array = {ARG.ARG_POL_subparties_affiliation = ARG_POL_party_no}
		}
	}
	clear_array = ARG_POL_active_parties_display
	for_each_loop = {
		array = ARG_POL_active_parties
		index = idx

		add_to_array = {ARG_POL_active_parties_display = ARG_POL_active_parties^idx}
	}
	add_to_array = {ARG_POL_active_parties_display = -1}
	every_owned_state = {
		limit = { has_state_flag = ARG_election_state }
		clear_array = ARG_POL_subparties_affiliation

		for_each_loop = {
			array = ARG.ARG_POL_subparties_affiliation
			index = idx

			add_to_array = {ARG_POL_subparties_affiliation = ARG.ARG_POL_subparties_affiliation^idx}
		}
	}
}

ARG_test_setup_seats = {
	every_owned_state = {
		limit = { has_state_flag = ARG_election_state }
		clear_array = ARG_state_party_seats
		add_to_array = { ARG_state_party_seats = 0 }
		resize_array = { ARG_state_party_seats = 8 }
		for_loop_effect = {
			end = ARG_state_seats
			random_list = {
				10 = {
					add_to_variable = { ARG_state_party_seats^0 = 1 }
				}
				10 = {
					add_to_variable = { ARG_state_party_seats^1 = 1 }
				}
				10 = {
					add_to_variable = { ARG_state_party_seats^2 = 1 }
				}
				10 = {
					add_to_variable = { ARG_state_party_seats^3 = 1 }
				}
				10 = {
					add_to_variable = { ARG_state_party_seats^4 = 1 }
				}
				10 = {
					add_to_variable = { ARG_state_party_seats^5 = 1 }
				}
				10 = {
					add_to_variable = { ARG_state_party_seats^6 = 1 }
				}
				10 = {
					add_to_variable = { ARG_state_party_seats^7 = 1 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	ARG_setup_congress_display = yes
}

ARG_setup_congress_display = {
	clear_array = ARG_frame_congress_array
	log = "------------"
	every_owned_state = {
		limit = { has_state_flag = ARG_election_state }
		clear_array = ARG_state_seats_display
		log = "STATE [This.GetName]"
		for_each_loop = {
			array = ARG_state_party_seats
			value = ARG_seats_value
			index = idx
			log = "S [This.GetName] ARG_seats_value:[?ARG_seats_value] idx:[?idx] ARG_state_party_seats^idx:[?ARG_state_party_seats^idx]"
			for_loop_effect = {
				end = ARG_state_party_seats^idx
				value = v
				set_temp_variable = { index = idx }
				add_to_temp_variable = { index = 1 }
				add_to_array = { ARG_state_seats_display = index }
				add_to_array = { ARG.ARG_frame_congress_array = index }
			}

		}
	}
}
ARG_POL_state_click_effect = {
	clr_country_flag = ARG_POL_GUI_senate_selected
	set_variable = {ARG_POL_state_congress_size = ARG_selected_state:ARG_state_deputies}
	set_variable = {ARG_POL_state_senate_size = ARG_selected_state:ARG_state_legislatures}

	set_variable = {ARG_POL_state_governor = ARG_selected_state:ARG_state_govenor}
	set_variable = {ARG_POL_state_governor_display = ARG_selected_state:ARG_state_governor_display}
	set_variable = {ARG_POL_state_governor_adjust = ARG_POL_state_governor}
	add_to_Variable = {ARG_POL_state_governor_adjust = -1}
	set_variable = {ARG_POL_current_state_senator_1 = ARG_selected_state:ARG_senator_1}
	set_variable = {ARG_POL_current_state_senator_2 = ARG_selected_state:ARG_senator_2}
	set_variable = {ARG_POL_current_state_senator_2_display = ARG_selected_state:ARG_senator_2_display}

	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {ARG_POL_state_senate_size = 0}
		}
		clr_country_flag = ARG_POL_GUI_senate_selected
	}
	clear_array = ARG_selected_states_to_set
	add_to_array = {ARG_selected_states_to_set = ARG_selected_state}
	for_each_scope_loop = {
		array = ARG_selected_states_to_set

		ARG_POL_GUI_update_state_leg_stuff = yes
	}
	for_each_loop = {
		array = ARG.ARG_POL_active_parties
		index = idx
		value = party_idx

		set_variable = {ARG_pie_var^party_idx = ARG_selected_state:ARG_endpoint_pres^party_idx}
	}
	#set_variable = {ps_pie_var = ARG_selected_state:ps_endpoint_pres}
	#set_variable = {ucrp_pie_var = ARG_selected_state:ucrp_endpoint_pres}
	#set_variable = {ucri_pie_var = ARG_selected_state:ucri_endpoint_pres}
	#set_variable = {pdp_pie_var = ARG_selected_state:pdp_endpoint_pres}
	#set_variable = {pdc_pie_var = ARG_selected_state:pdc_endpoint_pres}
	#set_variable = {prn_pie_var = ARG_selected_state:prn_endpoint_pres}
	#set_variable = {np_pie_var = ARG_selected_state:np_endpoint_pres}
	#set_variable = {fnpc_pie_var = ARG_selected_state:fnpc_endpoint_pres}

	clear_array = ARG_POL_state_other_parties
	clear_array = ARG_POL_state_other_parties_percentage
	clear_array = ARG_POL_state_other_parties_pres_points
	clear_array = ARG_POL_state_other_parties_frame

	for_each_loop = {
		array = ARG.ARG_POL_active_subparties
		index = idx
		value = party_idx

		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {idx = 0}
			}
			set_variable = {ARG_state_leading_party_percentage = ARG_selected_state:ARG_POL_state_party_percentage^idx}
			set_variable = {ARG_state_leading_party = ARG_selected_state:ARG_POL_state_party_index^idx}
			set_variable = {ARG_state_leading_party_pres_points = ARG_selected_state:ARG_POL_state_party_pres_points^idx}
			#add_to_variable = {ARG_state_leading_party = 1}
		}
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {ARG_selected_state:ARG_POL_state_party_pres_points^idx > 0}
				}
				add_to_array = {ARG_POL_state_other_parties = ARG_selected_state:ARG_POL_state_party_index^idx}
				add_to_array = {ARG_POL_state_other_parties_percentage = ARG_selected_state:ARG_POL_state_party_percentage^idx}
				add_to_array = {ARG_POL_state_other_parties_pres_points = ARG_selected_state:ARG_POL_state_party_pres_points^idx}
				#add_to_variable = {ARG_selected_state:ARG_POL_state_party_index^idx = 1}
				add_to_array = {ARG_POL_state_other_parties_frame = ARG_selected_state:ARG_POL_state_party_index^idx}
				#subtract_from_variable = {ARG_selected_state:ARG_POL_state_party_index^idx = 1}
			}
		}

		set_variable = {ARG_POL_selected_state_state_leg_vote_split^idx = ARG_selected_state:ARG_POL_percent_of_state_leg^idx}
	}
	ARG_update_states_state_leg_animation = yes
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = ARG_POL_GUI_senate_selected
		}
		ARG_POL_update_sens_amount_display = yes
	}
	else = {
		ARG_POL_update_deps_amount_display = yes
	}
}

		}
		clear_array = ARG_POL_GUI_cong_seat_x_glow
		clear_array = ARG_POL_GUI_cong_seat_y_glow
		clear_array = ARG_POL_GUI_sen_seat_x_glow
		clear_array = ARG_POL_GUI_sen_seat_y_glow
		for_loop_effect = {
			start = 0
			end = 100
			value = idx

			add_to_array = {ARG_POL_GUI_cong_seat_x_glow = ARG_POL_GUI_cong_seat_x^idx}
			add_to_array = {ARG_POL_GUI_cong_seat_y_glow = ARG_POL_GUI_cong_seat_y^idx}
			subtract_from_variable = {ARG_POL_GUI_cong_seat_x_glow^idx = 6}
			subtract_from_variable = {ARG_POL_GUI_cong_seat_y_glow^idx = 6}

			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {ARG_state_legislatures > 0}
				}
				add_to_array = {ARG_POL_GUI_sen_seat_x_glow = ARG_POL_GUI_sen_seat_x^idx}
				add_to_array = {ARG_POL_GUI_sen_seat_y_glow = ARG_POL_GUI_sen_seat_y^idx}
				subtract_from_variable = {ARG_POL_GUI_sen_seat_x_glow^idx = 6}
				subtract_from_variable = {ARG_POL_GUI_sen_seat_y_glow^idx = 6}
			}
		}
	}

	ARG_POL_GUI_highlight_state_leg_for_election = yes
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = cycle_1_sen_election
		}
		ARG_POL_GUI_highlight_all_cycle_1_sens = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = cycle_2_sen_election
		}
		ARG_POL_GUI_highlight_all_cycle_2_sens = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = cycle_3_sen_election
		}
		ARG_POL_GUI_highlight_all_cycle_3_sens = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = cycle_1_dep_election
		}
		ARG_POL_GUI_highlight_all_cycle_1_deps = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = cycle_2_dep_election
		}
		ARG_POL_GUI_highlight_all_cycle_2_deps = yes
	}
}
ARG_POL_update_party_pops_and_randomise = {
	every_owned_state = {
		limit = { has_state_flag = ARG_election_state }

		set_variable = {ARG_POL_state_total_pop = 0}
		for_each_loop = {
			array = ARG.ARG_POL_active_parties
			index = idx
			value = party_idx

			set_variable = {ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^party_idx = ARG_pol_party_pop^party_idx}
			randomize_variable = {
				var = ARG_poll_party_pop_multiplier
				distribution = uniform
				min = 0.9
				max = 1.1
			}
			multiply_variable = {ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^party_idx = ARG_poll_party_pop_multiplier}
			add_to_variable = {ARG_POL_state_total_pop = ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^party_idx}
		}

		for_each_loop = {
			array = ARG.ARG_POL_active_parties
			index = idx

			divide_variable = {ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^party_idx = ARG_POL_state_total_pop}
		}

		#set_variable = {ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^0 = ARG_pol_party_pop^0}

#

		#	end = 9
		#	value = idx
#
		#	randomize_variable = {
		#		var = ARG_poll_party_pop_multiplier
		#		distribution = uniform
		#		min = 0.9
		#		max = 1.1
		#	}
		#	multiply_variable = {ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^idx = ARG_poll_party_pop_multiplier}
		#}
#
		#set_variable = {ARG_POL_state_total_pop = ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^0}
		#add_to_variable = {ARG_POL_state_total_pop = ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^1}
		#add_to_variable = {ARG_POL_state_total_pop = ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^2}

		#add_to_variable = {ARG_POL_state_total_pop = ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^4}
		#add_to_variable = {ARG_POL_state_total_pop = ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^5}
		#add_to_variable = {ARG_POL_state_total_pop = ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^6}
		#add_to_variable = {ARG_POL_state_total_pop = ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^7}
		#add_to_variable = {ARG_POL_state_total_pop = ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^8}
#

		#divide_variable = {ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^1 = ARG_POL_state_total_pop}
		#divide_variable = {ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^2 = ARG_POL_state_total_pop}

		#divide_variable = {ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^5 = ARG_POL_state_total_pop}

ARG_POL_update_party_pops = {
	every_owned_state = {
		limit = { has_state_flag = ARG_election_state }

		set_variable = {ARG_POL_state_total_pop = 0}
		for_each_loop = {
			array = ARG.ARG_POL_active_parties
			index = idx
			value = party_idx

			add_to_variable = {ARG_POL_state_total_pop = ARG_pol_party_pop^party_idx}
			set_variable = {ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^party_idx = ARG_pol_party_pop^party_idx}
		}
		for_each_loop = {
			array = ARG.ARG_POL_active_parties
			index = idx
			value = party_idx

			divide_variable = {ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^party_idx = ARG_POL_state_total_pop}
		}

		#set_variable = {ARG_POL_state_total_pop = ARG_pol_party_pop^0}
		#add_to_variable = {ARG_POL_state_total_pop = ARG_pol_party_pop^1}
		#add_to_variable = {ARG_POL_state_total_pop = ARG_pol_party_pop^2}
		#add_to_variable = {ARG_POL_state_total_pop = ARG_pol_party_pop^3}
		#add_to_variable = {ARG_POL_state_total_pop = ARG_pol_party_pop^4}
		#add_to_variable = {ARG_POL_state_total_pop = ARG_pol_party_pop^5}
		#add_to_variable = {ARG_POL_state_total_pop = ARG_pol_party_pop^6}
		#add_to_variable = {ARG_POL_state_total_pop = ARG_pol_party_pop^7}
		#add_to_variable = {ARG_POL_state_total_pop = ARG_pol_party_pop^8}
#
		#set_variable = {ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^0 = ARG_pol_party_pop^0}
		#set_variable = {ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^1 = ARG_pol_party_pop^1}
		#set_variable = {ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^2 = ARG_pol_party_pop^2}
		#set_variable = {ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^3 = ARG_pol_party_pop^3}
		#set_variable = {ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^4 = ARG_pol_party_pop^4}
		#set_variable = {ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^5 = ARG_pol_party_pop^5}
		#set_variable = {ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^6 = ARG_pol_party_pop^6}
		#set_variable = {ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^7 = ARG_pol_party_pop^7}
		#set_variable = {ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^8 = ARG_pol_party_pop^8}

		#divide_variable = {ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^2 = ARG_POL_state_total_pop}

ARG_POL_remove_less_than_5 = {
	every_owned_state = {
		limit = { has_state_flag = ARG_election_state }

		clear_variable = ARG_POL_pop_to_distribute
		set_variable = {ARG_POL_num_of_parties_over_5 = ARG_POL_number_of_active_parties}

		for_each_loop = {
			array = ARG.ARG_POL_active_parties
			index = idx
			value = party_idx

			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^party_idx < 0.05}
				}
				add_to_variable = {ARG_POL_pop_to_distribute = ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^party_idx}
				add_to_variable = {ARG_POL_num_of_parties_over_5 = -1}
				set_variable = {ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^party_idx = 0}
			}
		}

		#for_loop_effect = {
		#	start = 0
		#	end = 8
		#	value = idx
#
		#	if = {
		#		limit = {
		#			check_variable = {ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^idx < 0.05}
		#		}
		#		add_to_variable = {ARG_POL_pop_to_distribute = ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^idx}
		#		add_to_variable = {ARG_POL_num_of_parties_over_5 = -1}
		#		set_variable = {ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^idx = 0}
		#	}
		#}
		divide_variable = {ARG_POL_pop_to_distribute = ARG_POL_num_of_parties_over_5}
		for_each_loop = {
			array = ARG.ARG_POL_active_parties
			index = idx
			value = party_idx

			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^party_idx > 0}
				}
				add_to_variable = {ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^party_idx = ARG_POL_pop_to_distribute}
			}
		}
		#for_loop_effect = {
		#	start = 0
		#	end = 8
		#	value = idx
#
		#	if = {
		#		limit = {
		#			check_variable = {ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^idx > 0}
		#		}
		#		add_to_variable = {ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^idx = ARG_POL_pop_to_distribute}
		#	}
		#}
	}
}

	clear_variable = FNPC_electoral_college_votes
	clear_variable = NP_electoral_college_votes
	clear_variable = PDP_electoral_college_votes
	clear_variable = PRN_electoral_college_votes
	clear_variable = OTHER_electoral_college_votes

	ARG_POL_update_party_pops = yes

	every_owned_state = {
		limit = { has_state_flag = ARG_election_state }

		for_each_loop = {
			array = ARG.ARG_POL_active_parties

			multiply_variable = {ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^party_idx = ARG_electoral_college_points}
			round_variable = ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^party_idx

		}

		#Multiply it by electoral college points#

		#round_variable = ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^1
		#round_variable = ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^2
		#round_variable = ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^3
		#round_variable = ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^4
		#round_variable = ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^5
		#round_variable = ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^6

ARG_POL_predict_presidential_election = {
	for_each_loop = {
		array = ARG_POL_active_parties
		index = idx
		value = party_idx

		clear_variable = ARG_electoral_college_votes_prediction^party_idx
	}
	#clear_variable = PS_electoral_college_votes_prediction
	#clear_variable = UCRP_electoral_college_votes_prediction
	#clear_variable = UCRI_electoral_college_votes_prediction
	#clear_variable = PDC_electoral_college_votes_prediction
	#clear_variable = FNPC_electoral_college_votes_prediction
	#clear_variable = NP_electoral_college_votes_prediction
	#clear_variable = PDP_electoral_college_votes_prediction
	#clear_variable = PRN_electoral_college_votes_prediction
	#clear_variable = OTHER_electoral_college_votes_prediction

	ARG_POL_update_party_pops_and_randomise = yes

	clear_array = ARG_POL_country_array_for_sorting
	for_each_loop = {
		array = ARG_POL_active_parties
		index = idx

		random_country = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					is_in_array = {ARG.ARG_POL_country_array_for_sorting = THIS}
				}
			}
			add_to_array = {ARG.ARG_POL_country_array_for_sorting = THIS}
		}
	}
	#add_to_array = {ARG_POL_country_array_for_sorting = ARG}
	#add_to_array = {ARG_POL_country_array_for_sorting = BRA}
	#add_to_array = {ARG_POL_country_array_for_sorting = USA}
	#add_to_array = {ARG_POL_country_array_for_sorting = CAN}
	#add_to_array = {ARG_POL_country_array_for_sorting = GER}
	#add_to_array = {ARG_POL_country_array_for_sorting = CHL}
	#add_to_array = {ARG_POL_country_array_for_sorting = PRU}
	#add_to_array = {ARG_POL_country_array_for_sorting = BOL}
	#add_to_array = {ARG_POL_country_array_for_sorting = MEX}

	every_owned_state = {
		limit = { has_state_flag = ARG_election_state }

		clear_variable = ARG_previous_endpoint
		for_each_loop = {
			array = ARG.ARG_POL_active_parties
			index = idx
			value = party_idx

			randomize_variable = {
				var = ARG_poll_party_pop_multiplier
				distribution = uniform
				min = 0.9
				max = 1.1
			}

			multiply_variable = {ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^party_idx = ARG_poll_party_pop_multiplier}
			set_variable = {ARG_POL_pres_predicted_percent^party_idx = ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^party_idx}
			divide_variable = {ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^party_idx = 100}
			multiply_variable = {ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^party_idx = ARG_electoral_college_points}
			round_variable = ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^party_idx
			add_to_variable = {ARG.ARG_electoral_college_votes_prediction^party_idx = ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^party_idx}

			set_variable = {ARG_endpoint_pres^party_idx = ARG_previous_endpoint}
			add_to_variable = {ARG_endpoint_pres^party_idx = ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^party_idx}
			set_variable = {ARG_previous_endpoint = ARG_endpoint_pres^party_idx}
			divide_variable = {ARG_endpoint_pres^party_idx = ARG_electoral_college_points}
			multiply_variable = {ARG_endpoint_pres^party_idx = 100}

			###########################################################################

			set_variable = {ARG_POL_country_array = ARG.ARG_POL_country_array_for_sorting^idx}
			set_variable = {ARG_POL_country_array:ARG_state_pop_for_sorting = ARG_POL_pres_predicted_percent^party_idx}
			set_variable = {ARG_POL_country_array:ARG_index_value = party_idx}
			set_variable = {ARG_POL_country_array:ARG_pres_points_value = ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^party_idx}
		}

		#Multiply it by electoral college points#
		#multiply_variable = {ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^0 = ARG_electoral_college_points}
		#multiply_variable = {ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^1 = ARG_electoral_college_points}
		#multiply_variable = {ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^2 = ARG_electoral_college_points}
		#multiply_variable = {ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^3 = ARG_electoral_college_points}
		#multiply_variable = {ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^4 = ARG_electoral_college_points}
		#multiply_variable = {ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^5 = ARG_electoral_college_points}
		#multiply_variable = {ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^6 = ARG_electoral_college_points}
		#multiply_variable = {ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^7 = ARG_electoral_college_points}
		#multiply_variable = {ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^8 = ARG_electoral_college_points}
#
		#round_variable = ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^0
		#round_variable = ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^1
		#round_variable = ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^2
		#round_variable = ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^3
		#round_variable = ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^4
		#round_variable = ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^5
		#round_variable = ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^6
		#round_variable = ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^7
		#round_variable = ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^8
#
		#add_to_variable = {ARG.PS_electoral_college_votes_prediction = ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^0}
		#add_to_variable = {ARG.UCRP_electoral_college_votes_prediction = ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^1}
		#add_to_variable = {ARG.UCRI_electoral_college_votes_prediction = ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^2}
		#add_to_variable = {ARG.PDC_electoral_college_votes_prediction = ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^3}
		#add_to_variable = {ARG.FNPC_electoral_college_votes_prediction = ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^4}
		#add_to_variable = {ARG.NP_electoral_college_votes_prediction = ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^5}
		#add_to_variable = {ARG.PDP_electoral_college_votes_prediction = ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^6}
		#add_to_variable = {ARG.PRN_electoral_college_votes_prediction = ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^7}
		#add_to_variable = {ARG.OTHER_electoral_college_votes_prediction = ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^8}

		#set_variable = {ps_endpoint_pres = ARG_POL_pres_predicted_percent^0}
#
		#set_variable = {ucrp_endpoint_pres = ps_endpoint_pres}
		#add_to_variable = {ucrp_endpoint_pres = ARG_POL_pres_predicted_percent^1}
#
		#set_variable = {ucri_endpoint_pres = ucrp_endpoint_pres}
		#add_to_variable = {ucri_endpoint_pres = ARG_POL_pres_predicted_percent^2}
#
		#set_variable = {pdc_endpoint_pres = ucri_endpoint_pres}
		#add_to_variable = {pdc_endpoint_pres = ARG_POL_pres_predicted_percent^3}
#
		#set_variable = {fnpc_endpoint_pres = pdc_endpoint_pres}
		#add_to_variable = {fnpc_endpoint_pres = ARG_POL_pres_predicted_percent^4}
#
		#set_variable = {np_endpoint_pres = fnpc_endpoint_pres}
		#add_to_variable = {np_endpoint_pres = ARG_POL_pres_predicted_percent^5}
#
		#set_variable = {pdp_endpoint_pres = np_endpoint_pres}
		#add_to_variable = {pdp_endpoint_pres = ARG_POL_pres_predicted_percent^6}
#
		#set_variable = {prn_endpoint_pres = pdp_endpoint_pres}
		#add_to_variable = {prn_endpoint_pres = ARG_POL_pres_predicted_percent^7}

		#for_loop_effect = {
		#	start = 0
		#	end = 9
		#	value = idx
#
		#	set_variable = {ARG_POL_country_array = ARG.ARG_POL_country_array_for_sorting^idx}
		#	set_variable = {ARG_POL_country_array:ARG_state_pop_for_sorting = ARG_POL_pres_predicted_percent^idx}
		#	set_variable = {ARG_POL_country_array:ARG_index_value = idx}
		#	set_variable = {ARG_POL_country_array:ARG_pres_points_value = ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^idx}
		#}

		ARG = {
			get_sorted_scored_countries = {
				scorer = TNO_ARG_presidential_state_scorer
				array = sorted_percent_state_pres
			}
		}

		clear_array = ARG.current_state_pop_score
		clear_array = ARG.current_state_index
		clear_array = ARG.current_state_pres_points_value

		for_each_scope_loop = {
			array = ARG.sorted_percent_state_pres

			add_to_array = {ARG.current_state_pop_score = ARG_state_pop_for_sorting}
			add_to_array = {ARG.current_state_index = ARG_index_value}
			add_to_array = {ARG.current_state_pres_points_value = ARG_pres_points_value}
		}
		for_each_loop = {
			array = ARG.ARG_POL_active_parties
			index = idx
			value = party_idx

			set_variable = {ARG_POL_state_party_percentage^idx = ARG.current_state_pop_score^idx}
			set_variable = {ARG_POL_state_party_index^idx = ARG.current_state_index^idx}
			set_variable = {ARG_POL_state_party_pres_points^idx = ARG.current_state_pres_points_value^idx}
		}

	}
	clear_variable = ARG_total_elec_votes_prediction
	for_each_loop = {
		array = ARG_POL_active_parties
		index = idx
		value = party_idx

		add_to_variable = {ARG_total_elec_votes_prediction = ARG_electoral_college_votes_prediction^party_idx}
		set_variable = {electoral_college_percent_prediction^party_idx = ARG_electoral_college_votes_prediction^party_idx}
	}
	#set_variable = {ARG_total_elec_votes_prediction = PS_electoral_college_votes_prediction}
	#add_to_variable = {ARG_total_elec_votes_prediction = UCRP_electoral_college_votes_prediction}
	#add_to_variable = {ARG_total_elec_votes_prediction = UCRI_electoral_college_votes_prediction}
	#add_to_variable = {ARG_total_elec_votes_prediction = PDC_electoral_college_votes_prediction}
	#add_to_variable = {ARG_total_elec_votes_prediction = FNPC_electoral_college_votes_prediction}
	#add_to_variable = {ARG_total_elec_votes_prediction = NP_electoral_college_votes_prediction}
	#add_to_variable = {ARG_total_elec_votes_prediction = PDP_electoral_college_votes_prediction}
	#add_to_variable = {ARG_total_elec_votes_prediction = PRN_electoral_college_votes_prediction}
	#add_to_variable = {ARG_total_elec_votes_prediction = OTHER_electoral_college_votes_prediction}
#
	#set_variable = {electoral_college_percent_prediction^0 = PS_electoral_college_votes_prediction}
	#set_variable = {electoral_college_percent_prediction^1 = UCRP_electoral_college_votes_prediction}
	#set_variable = {electoral_college_percent_prediction^2 = UCRI_electoral_college_votes_prediction}
	#set_variable = {electoral_college_percent_prediction^3 = PDC_electoral_college_votes_prediction}
	#set_variable = {electoral_college_percent_prediction^4 = FNPC_electoral_college_votes_prediction}
	#set_variable = {electoral_college_percent_prediction^5 = NP_electoral_college_votes_prediction}
	#set_variable = {electoral_college_percent_prediction^6 = PDP_electoral_college_votes_prediction}
	#set_variable = {electoral_college_percent_prediction^7 = PRN_electoral_college_votes_prediction}
	#set_variable = {electoral_college_percent_prediction^8 = OTHER_electoral_college_votes_prediction}

	for_each_loop = {
		array = ARG_POL_active_parties
		index = idx
		value = party_idx

		divide_variable = {electoral_college_percent_prediction^party_idx = ARG_total_elec_votes_prediction}
		multiply_variable = {electoral_college_percent_prediction^party_idx = 100}
		round_variable = electoral_college_percent_prediction^party_idx
		set_variable = {ARG_country_tag_sorting = ARG_POL_country_array_for_sorting^idx}
		set_variable = {ARG_country_tag_sorting:ARG_pres_sorting_var = electoral_college_percent_prediction^party_idx}
		set_variable = {ARG_country_tag_sorting:ARG_pres_index_value = party_idx}
	}

	get_sorted_scored_countries = {
		scorer = TNO_ARG_presidential_scorer
		array = ARG.sorted_scores_pres
	}
	clear_array = electoral_college_percent_prediction
	clear_array = ARG_pres_bars
	for_each_scope_loop = {
		array = sorted_scores_pres

		set_variable = {ARG.ARG_POL_final_bit = ARG_pres_index_value}
		#add_to_variable = {ARG.ARG_POL_final_bit = 1}
		multiply_variable = {ARG.ARG_POL_final_bit = 1000}
		add_to_variable = {ARG_pres_sorting_var = ARG.ARG_POL_final_bit}
		add_to_array = {ARG.ARG_pres_bars = ARG_pres_index_value}
		add_to_array = {ARG.electoral_college_percent_prediction = ARG_pres_sorting_var}
	}
	clear_array = ARG_other_major_candidates
	clear_array = ARG_other_major_candidates_votes
	for_loop_effect = {
		start = 0
		end = 4
		value = idx

		set_temp_variable = {ARG_index_value = electoral_college_percent_prediction^idx}
		divide_temp_variable = {ARG_index_value = 1000}
		round_temp_variable = ARG_index_value
		multiply_temp_variable = {ARG_index_value = 1000}
		set_temp_variable = {ARG_percent_value = electoral_college_percent_prediction^idx}
		subtract_from_temp_variable = {ARG_percent_value = ARG_index_value}
		divide_temp_variable = {ARG_index_value = 1000}
		divide_temp_variable = {ARG_percent_value = 100}
		multiply_temp_variable = {ARG_percent_value = ARG_total_elec_votes_prediction}
		round_temp_variable = ARG_percent_value

		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {idx = 0}
			}
			set_variable = {ARG_leading_candidate = ARG_index_value}
			set_variable = {ARG_POL_GUI_leading_party_votes = ARG_percent_value}
		}
		else = {
			add_to_array = {ARG_other_major_candidates = ARG_index_value}
			add_to_array = {ARG_other_major_candidates_votes = ARG_percent_value}
		}
	}
}
ARG_POL_randomise_pops_for_polls = {
	every_owned_state = {
		limit = {
			has_state_flag = ARG_election_state
		}
		for_each_loop = {
			array = ARG.ARG_POL_active_subparties
			index = idx
			value = party_idx

			randomize_variable = {
				var = ARG_poll_party_pop_multiplier
				distribution = uniform
				min = 0.9
				max = 1.1
			}
			multiply_variable = {ARG_POL_sub_party_deps_state_change^party_idx = ARG_poll_party_pop_multiplier}
		}
	}
}

ARG_POL_hold_cycle_1_deps_election = {
	ARG_POL_save_current_elections_deps_count = yes
	ARG_POL_pops_for_deps_setup = yes

	every_owned_state = {
		limit = {
			has_state_flag = ARG_election_state
			has_state_flag = cycle_1_dep_election
		}
		clear_variable = ARG_POL_total_deps_elected
		for_each_loop = {
			array = ARG.ARG_POL_active_subparties
			index = idx
			value = party_idx

ARG_POL_update_national_deps_prediction = {
	for_each_loop = {
		array = ARG_POL_active_subparties
		index = idx
		value = party_idx

		clear_variable = ARG_POL_num_of_cycle_1_deps_prediction^party_idx
		clear_variable = ARG_POL_num_of_cycle_1_deps_prediction^party_idx
		clear_variable = ARG_POL_total_num_of_deps_predicted^party_idx
	}
	for_each_loop = {
		array = ARG_POL_active_parties
		index = idx
		value = party_idx

		clear_variable = ARG_total_deps_predicted^party_idx
	}

	#clear_variable = PS_total_deps_predicted
	#clear_variable = UCRP_total_deps_predicted
	#clear_variable = UCRI_total_deps_predicted
	#clear_variable = PDC_total_deps_predicted
	#clear_variable = FNPC_total_deps_predicted

	#clear_variable = PDP_total_deps_predicted

	every_owned_state = {

		for_each_loop = {

			clear_variable = ARG_total_deps_state_predicted^party_idx
		}

		if = {

			ARG = {
				clr_country_flag = ARG_cycle_1_election
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				ARG = {
					has_country_flag = ARG_cycle_2_election
				}
			}

				index = idx
				value = party_idx

			}

				clr_country_flag = ARG_cycle_2_election
			}

		clear_variable = ARG.ARG_deps_predicted_in_total

			array = ARG.ARG_POL_active_subparties
			index = idx
			value = party_idx

			add_to_variable = {ARG.ARG_POL_num_of_cycle_1_deps_predicted^party_idx = ARG_POL_deps_state_prediction_cycle_1^party_idx}
			add_to_variable = {ARG.ARG_POL_num_of_cycle_2_deps_predicted^party_idx = ARG_POL_deps_state_prediction_cycle_2^party_idx}

			add_to_variable = {ARG.ARG_POL_total_num_of_deps_predicted^party_idx = ARG_POL_deps_state_prediction_cycle_1^party_idx}
			add_to_variable = {ARG.ARG_POL_total_num_of_deps_predicted^party_idx = ARG_POL_deps_state_prediction_cycle_2^party_idx}

			set_variable = {ARG_POL_total_deps_in_state_predicted^party_idx = ARG_POL_deps_state_prediction_cycle_1^party_idx}
			add_to_variable = {ARG_POL_total_deps_in_state_predicted^party_idx = ARG_POL_deps_state_prediction_cycle_2^party_idx}

			set_variable = {target_party = ARG_POL_subparties_affiliation^party_idx}
			add_to_variable = {ARG_total_deps_state_predicted^target_party = ARG_POL_deps_state_prediction_cycle_1^party_idx}
			add_to_variable = {ARG_total_deps_state_predicted^target_party = ARG_POL_deps_state_prediction_cycle_2^party_idx}

			set_variable = {ARG_POL_deps_predicted_change^party_idx = ARG_POL_total_num_of_deps_predicted^party_idx}
			subtract_from_variable = {ARG_POL_deps_predicted_change^party_idx = ARG_POL_total_num_of_deps^party_idx}

			add_to_variable = {ARG.ARG_deps_predicted_in_total = ARG.ARG_POL_total_num_of_deps_predicted^idx}
		}
		for_each_loop = {
			array = ARG.ARG_POL_active_parties
			index = idx
			value = party_idx

			add_to_variable = {ARG.ARG_total_deps_predicted^party_idx = ARG_total_deps_state_predicted^party_idx}
			set_variable = {ARG_total_party_state_deps_predicted^party_idx = ARG_total_deps_state_predicted^party_idx}
		}

	for_each_loop = {
		array = ARG_POL_active_subparties
		index = idx
		value = party_idx

		clear_variable = ARG_POL_num_of_cycle_1_deps^party_idx
		clear_variable = ARG_POL_num_of_cycle_2_deps^party_idx
		clear_variable = ARG_POL_total_num_of_deps^party_idx
	}

	for_each_loop = {
		array = ARG_POL_active_parties
		index = idx
		value = party_idx

	}

			has_state_flag = ARG_election_state
		}

		for_each_loop = {
			array = ARG.ARG_POL_active_parties

ARG_POL_sort_out_state_funnies_for_deps = {
	###ffs why is Argentina so confusing###
	#state by fucking state#
	1506 = { #La Pampa
		if = {
			limit = {
				ARG = {
					has_country_flag = MPP_banned
				}
			}
			set_variable = {ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^5 = 0} #If MPP banned then unorganised and will vote blank
		}
	}
	1508 = { #Rio Negro
		if = {
			limit = {
				ARG = {
					has_country_flag = APN_banned
				}
			}
			set_variable = {ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^5 = 0} #If APN banned then unorganised and will vote blank
		}
	}
	1507 = { #Neuquen
		if = {
			limit = {
				ARG = {
					has_country_flag = PJ_banned
				}
			}
			set_variable = {ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^7 = 0} #If PJ banned then unorganised and will vote blank
		}
		add_to_variable = {ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^4 = ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^6}
		set_variable = {ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^6 = 0} #PDP run for FNPC
	}
	1509 = { #Chubut
		add_to_variable = {ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^4 = ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^6}
		set_variable = {ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^6 = 0} #PDP run for FNPC
	}
	1504 = { #San Juan
		add_to_variable = {ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^4 = ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^6}
		set_variable = {ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^6 = 0} #PDP run for FNPC

		add_to_variable = {ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^5 = ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^0}
		set_variable = {ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^0 = 0} #For some reason, the PS in San Juan was merged with the UCR-B (NP)
	}
	1499 = { #Chaco
		if = {
			limit = {
				ARG = {
					has_country_flag = APC_banned
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = {ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^4 = ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^5}
			set_variable = {ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^5 = 0} #For some reason, the NP runs with the FNPC if APC is banned
		}
	}
	1496 = { #Catamarca
		if = {
			limit = {
				ARG = {
					has_country_flag = PJ_banned
				}
			}
			set_variable = {ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^7 = 0} #If PJ banned then unorganised and will vote blank
		}
	}
	1498 = { #Formosa
		if = {
			limit = {
				ARG = {
					has_country_flag = PJ_banned
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = {ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^2 = ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^7}
			set_variable = {ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^7 = 0} #If PJ is banned then they vote for the UCRI for whatever reason
		}
		add_to_variable = {ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^3 = ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^5}
		set_variable = {ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^5 = 0} #As well the NP runs with the PDC here (FFS Argentina)
	}
	1495 = { #Salta
		if = {
			limit = {
				ARG = {
					has_country_flag = PJ_banned
				}
			}
			set_variable = {ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^7 = 0} #If PJ is banned then unorganized and will vote blank
		}
	}
	1500 = { #Misiones
		if = {
			limit = {
				ARG = {
					has_country_flag = PJ_banned
				}
			}
			set_variable = {ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^7 = 0} #If PJ is banned then unorganized and will vote blank
		}
		set_variable = {ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^5 = 0} #NP just flat out aren't organised here and vote blank

		add_to_variable = {ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^4 = ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^6}
		set_variable = {ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^6 = 0} #PDP run for FNPC
	}
	1497 = { #La Rioja
		if = {
			limit = {
				ARG = {
					has_country_flag = PJ_banned
				}
			}
			set_variable = {ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^7 = ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^5} #If PJ is banned then unorganized and will vote blank, but the NP will vote for the UP which is a PRN party?
			set_variable = {multiplier_prn_up = 1}
		}
	}
	#Now we recalculate the percentages with all the funnies included
	every_owned_state = {
		limit = {
			has_state_flag = ARG_election_state
		}
		clear_variable = ARG_POL_total_funnies
		for_each_loop = {
			array = ARG.ARG_POL_active_parties
			index = idx
			value = party_idx

			add_to_variable = {ARG_POL_total_funnies = ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^party_idx}
		}
		for_each_loop = {
			array = ARG.ARG_POL_active_parties
			index = idx
			value = party_idx

			divide_variable = {ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^party_idx = ARG_POL_total_funnies}
		}
		#set_variable = {ARG_POL_total_funnies = ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^0}
		#add_to_variable = {ARG_POL_total_funnies = ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^1}
		#add_to_variable = {ARG_POL_total_funnies = ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^2}
		#add_to_variable = {ARG_POL_total_funnies = ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^3}
		#add_to_variable = {ARG_POL_total_funnies = ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^4}
		#add_to_variable = {ARG_POL_total_funnies = ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^5}
		#add_to_variable = {ARG_POL_total_funnies = ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^6}
		#add_to_variable = {ARG_POL_total_funnies = ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^7}
		#add_to_variable = {ARG_POL_total_funnies = ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^8}
#
		#divide_variable = {ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^0 = ARG_POL_total_funnies}
		#divide_variable = {ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^1 = ARG_POL_total_funnies}
		#divide_variable = {ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^2 = ARG_POL_total_funnies}
		#divide_variable = {ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^3 = ARG_POL_total_funnies}
		#divide_variable = {ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^4 = ARG_POL_total_funnies}
		#divide_variable = {ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^5 = ARG_POL_total_funnies}
		#divide_variable = {ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^6 = ARG_POL_total_funnies}
		#divide_variable = {ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^7 = ARG_POL_total_funnies}
		#divide_variable = {ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^8 = ARG_POL_total_funnies}
	}
}
ARG_POL_sortout_seats_map = {
	every_owned_state = {
		limit = {
			has_state_flag = ARG_election_state
		}
		clear_variable = ARG_previous_startpoint

		###########################################################
		clear_array = ARG_state_seats_display
		resize_array = { ARG_state_seats_display = ARG_state_seats }
		###########################################################

		for_each_loop = {
			array = ARG.ARG_POL_active_parties
			index = idx
			value = party_idx

			set_variable = {ARG_startpoint^party_idx = ARG_previous_startpoint}
			add_to_variable = {ARG_startpoint^party_idx = ARG_total_deps_state^party_idx}

			for_loop_effect = {
				start = ARG_previous_startpoint
				end = ARG_startpoint^party_idx
				value = jdx

				set_variable = { ARG_state_seats_display^jdx = party_idx }
				set_variable = { ARG_state_seats_display_tt^jdx = party_idx }
			}
			set_variable = {ARG_previous_startpoint = ARG_startpoint^party_idx}
		}

ARG_POL_display_states_seat_animation = {
	clear_array = ARG_running_tally_array
	clear_variable = ARG_running_tally_variable
	add_to_array = {ARG_running_tally_array = 0}
	for_each_loop = {
		array = ARG.ARG_POL_active_subparties
		index = idx
		value = party_idx

		add_to_variable = {ARG_running_tally_variable = ARG_POL_total_num_of_deps^party_idx}
		add_to_array = {ARG_running_tally_array = ARG_running_tally_variable}
	}
	every_owned_state = {
		limit = {
			has_state_flag = ARG_election_state
		}
		clear_array = ARG_map_seat_value
		clear_array = ARG_running_tally_array
		for_each_loop = {
			array = ARG.ARG_running_tally_array
			index = idx
			value = tally_value


			add_to_array = {ARG_running_tally_array = tally_value}
		}
		for_each_loop = {
			array = ARG_state_seats_display
			index = idx

			set_variable = {ARG_state_adjusted_value = ARG_POL_GUI_dep_seat_subparty^idx}
			add_to_variable = {ARG_running_tally_array^ARG_state_adjusted_value = 1}
			add_to_array = {ARG_map_seat_value = ARG_running_tally_array^ARG_state_adjusted_value}
			multiply_variable = {ARG_map_seat_value^idx = 1000}
			add_to_variable = {ARG_map_seat_value^idx = 194}
			multiply_variable = {ARG_map_seat_value^idx = 10}
			add_to_variable = {ARG_map_seat_value^idx = ARG_state_seats_display^idx}
		}
		for_each_loop = {
			array = ARG.ARG_POL_active_subparties
			index = idx
			value = party_idx

			set_variable = {ARG.ARG_running_tally_array^idx = ARG_running_tally_array^party_idx}
		}
	}
}
ARG_POL_sortout_congress = {
	clear_variable = ARG_endpoint_previous
	clear_variable = ARG_deps_counter
	for_each_loop = {
		array = ARG_POL_active_parties
		index = idx
		value = party_idx

		set_variable = {ARG_startpoint^party_idx = ARG_endpoint_previous}
		add_to_variable = {ARG_startpoint^party_idx = ARG_total_deps^party_idx}
		set_variable = {ARG_target_party = party_idx}
		for_loop_effect = {
			start = ARG_endpoint_previous
			end = ARG_startpoint^party_idx
			value = jdx

			add_to_variable = {ARG_deps_counter = 1}
			set_variable = {ARG_frame_congress_array^jdx = ARG_deps_counter}
			multiply_variable = {ARG_frame_congress_array^jdx = 1000}
			add_to_variable = {ARG_frame_congress_array^jdx = 194}
			multiply_variable = {ARG_frame_congress_array^jdx = 10}
			add_to_variable = {ARG_frame_congress_array^jdx = ARG_target_party}
			set_variable = {ARG_frame_congress_array_loc^jdx = ARG_target_party}
		}
		set_variable = {ARG_endpoint_previous = ARG_startpoint^party_idx}
	}
	#set_variable = {ucri_startpoint = PS_total_deps}

	#add_to_variable = {other_endpoint = OTHER_total_deps}

ARG_POL_update_state_deps_display = {
	clear_array = ARG_POL_states_display_national
	clear_variable = ARG_POL_state_deps_running_total
	for_each_loop = {
		array = ARG.ARG_POL_active_subparties
		index = idx
		value = party_idx

		add_to_array = {ARG_POL_states_display_national = ARG_POL_state_deps_running_total}
		add_to_variable = {ARG_POL_state_deps_running_total = ARG_legs_in_state_dep^party_idx}
		multiply_variable = {ARG_POL_states_display_national^idx = 100}
		add_to_variable = {ARG_POL_states_display_national^idx = ARG_legs_in_state_dep^party_idx}
		multiply_variable = {ARG_POL_states_display_national^idx = 100}
		add_to_variable = {ARG_POL_states_display_national^idx = ARG_state_deputies}
	}
}
ARG_POL_update_state_sens_display = {
	clear_array = ARG_POL_states_display_sens_national
	clear_variable = ARG_POL_state_sens_running_total
	for_each_loop = {
		array = ARG.ARG_POL_active_subparties
		index = idx
		value = party_idx

		add_to_array = {ARG_POL_states_display_sens_national = ARG_POL_state_sens_running_total}
		add_to_variable = {ARG_POL_state_sens_running_total = ARG_legs_in_state_sen^party_idx}
		multiply_variable = {ARG_POL_states_display_sens_national^party_idx = 100}
		add_to_variable = {ARG_POL_states_display_sens_national^party_idx = ARG_legs_in_state_sen^party_idx}
		multiply_variable = {ARG_POL_states_display_sens_national^party_idx = 100}
		add_to_variable = {ARG_POL_states_display_sens_national^party_idx = ARG_state_legislatures}
	}
}
ARG_POL_update_deps_amount_display = {
	for_each_loop = {
		array = ARG_POL_active_parties
		index = idx
		value = party_idx

		set_variable = {ARG_state = party_idx}
		clear_array = ARG_state:ARG_POL_total_deps_number_display_state
	}
	for_each_loop = {
		array = ARG_POL_active_subparties
		index = idx
		value = party_idx

		set_variable = {ARG_state_add = ARG_POL_subparties_affiliation^party_idx}
		add_to_array = {ARG_state_add:ARG_POL_total_deps_number_display_state = ARG_selected_state:ARG_POL_states_display_national^party_idx}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {ARG_selected_state:ARG_POL_GUI_display_seat_animation_deps = 0}
		}
		set_variable = {ARG_selected_state:ARG_POL_GUI_display_seat_animation_deps = 1}
		ARG_update_states_state_leg_animation = yes
	}
}
ARG_POL_update_sens_amount_display = {
	for_each_loop = {
		array = ARG.ARG_POL_active_parties
		index = idx
		value = party_idx

		set_variable = {ARG_state = party_idx}
		clear_array = ARG_state:ARG_POL_total_deps_number_display_state

		array = ARG.ARG_POL_active_subparties
		index = idx
		value = party_idx

		set_variable = {ARG_state_add = ARG_POL_subparties_affiliation^party_idx}
		add_to_array = {ARG_state_add:ARG_POL_total_deps_number_display_state = ARG_selected_state:ARG_POL_states_display_sens_national^party_idx}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {ARG_selected_state:ARG_POL_GUI_display_seat_animation_sens = 0}
		}
		set_variable = {ARG_selected_state:ARG_POL_GUI_display_seat_animation_sens = 1}
		ARG_update_states_state_leg_animation = yes
	}
}

ARG_POL_update_deps_animation = {
	add_to_variable = {ARG_pol_deps_animation_update = 1}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {ARG_pol_deps_animation_update = 2}
		}
		set_variable = {ARG_pol_deps_animation_update = 0}
	}
}
ARG_POL_update_deps_count_animation = {
	add_to_variable = {ARG_pol_deps_animation_count_update = 1}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {ARG_pol_deps_animation_count_update = 2}
		}
		set_variable = {ARG_pol_deps_animation_count_update = 0}
	}
}
ARG_POL_63_deps_election = { #Yep, just why Argentina. Just Why?
	ARG_POL_save_current_elections_deps_count = yes
	ARG_POL_pops_for_deps_setup = yes

	every_owned_state = {
		limit = {
			has_state_flag = ARG_election_state
		}
		#Winner gets 2/3 of the deps and runner up gets 1/3
		set_variable = {ARG_num_of_deps_for_winner = ARG_no_of_cycle_1_deputies}
		add_to_variable = {ARG_num_of_deps_for_winner = ARG_no_of_cycle_2_deputies}
		set_variable = {ARG_num_of_deps_for_second = ARG_num_of_deps_for_winner}
		multiply_variable = {ARG_num_of_deps_for_winner = 0.666}
		multiply_variable = {ARG_num_of_deps_for_second = 0.333}
		round_variable = ARG_num_of_deps_for_winner
		round_variable = ARG_num_of_deps_for_second

		#We need to calculate the split between cycle 1 and cycle 2 reps#
		#3 conditions, if either are 0 and if neither are 0#
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {ARG_no_of_cycle_1_deputies = 0}
			}
			set_variable = {ARG_cycle_2_split = 1}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {ARG_no_of_cycle_2_deputies = 0}
			}
			set_variable = {ARG_cycle_1_split = 1}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {ARG_no_of_cycle_1_deputies > 0}
				check_variable = {ARG_no_of_cycle_2_deputies > 0}
			}
			set_variable = {ARG_total_deps_in_this_state = ARG_no_of_cycle_1_deputies}
			add_to_variable = {ARG_total_deps_in_this_state = ARG_no_of_cycle_2_deputies}
			set_variable = {ARG_cycle_1_split = ARG_no_of_cycle_1_deputies}
			set_variable = {ARG_cycle_2_split = ARG_no_of_cycle_2_deputies}
			divide_variable = {ARG_cycle_1_split = ARG_total_deps_in_this_state}
			divide_variable = {ARG_cycle_2_split = ARG_total_deps_in_this_state}
		}

		clear_array = ARG_POL_all_parties_in_state
		for_each_loop = {
			array = ARG.ARG_POL_active_subparties
			index = idx
			value = party_idx

			add_to_array = {ARG_POL_all_parties_in_state = ARG_POL_sub_party_deps_state_change^party_idx}
		}
		find_highest_in_array = { array = ARG_POL_all_parties_in_state }
		set_variable = {ARG_POL_deps_state_cycle_1^i = ARG_num_of_deps_for_winner}
		set_variable = {ARG_POL_deps_state_cycle_2^i = ARG_num_of_deps_for_winner}
		multiply_variable = {ARG_POL_deps_state_cycle_1^i = ARG_cycle_1_split}
		multiply_variable = {ARG_POL_deps_state_cycle_2^i = ARG_cycle_2_split}
		round_variable = ARG_POL_deps_state_cycle_1^i
		round_variable = ARG_POL_deps_state_cycle_2^i
		set_variable = {ARG_deps_total_elected_for_state_cycle_1 = ARG_POL_deps_state_cycle_1^i}
		set_variable = {ARG_deps_total_elected_for_state_cycle_2 = ARG_POL_deps_state_cycle_2^i}

		set_variable = {ARG_POL_all_parties_in_state^i = 0}

		find_highest_in_array = { array = ARG_POL_all_parties_in_state }
		set_variable = {ARG_POL_deps_state_cycle_1^i = ARG_num_of_deps_for_second}
		set_variable = {ARG_POL_deps_state_cycle_2^i = ARG_num_of_deps_for_second}
		multiply_variable = {ARG_POL_deps_state_cycle_1^i = ARG_cycle_1_split}
		multiply_variable = {ARG_POL_deps_state_cycle_2^i = ARG_cycle_2_split}
		round_variable = ARG_POL_deps_state_cycle_1^i
		round_variable = ARG_POL_deps_state_cycle_2^i
		add_to_variable = {ARG_deps_total_elected_for_state_cycle_1 = ARG_POL_deps_state_cycle_1^i}
		add_to_variable = {ARG_deps_total_elected_for_state_cycle_2 = ARG_POL_deps_state_cycle_2^i}



		#Finally just need to run a check to make sure no-one has more than they should#
		ARG_POL_check_for_extra_deps = yes

		#Since this is meant to be a fresh election then we can do set then add#
		for_each_loop = {
			array = ARG.ARG_POL_active_subparties
			index = idx
			value = party_idx

			set_variable = {ARG_POL_deps_state^party_idx = ARG_POL_deps_state_cycle_1^party_idx}
			add_to_variable = {ARG_POL_deps_state^party_idx = ARG_POL_deps_state_cycle_2^party_idx}
		}

	ARG_POL_update_amount_of_deps_nationally = yes

}
ARG_POL_63_deps_election_prediction = {
	ARG_POL_pops_for_deps_setup = yes

	ARG_POL_randomise_pops_for_polls = yes

	every_owned_state = {
		limit = {
			has_state_flag = ARG_election_state
		}
		#Winner gets 2/3 of the deps and runner up gets 1/3
		set_variable = {ARG_num_of_deps_for_winner = ARG_no_of_cycle_1_deputies}
		add_to_variable = {ARG_num_of_deps_for_winner = ARG_no_of_cycle_2_deputies}
		set_variable = {ARG_num_of_deps_for_second = ARG_num_of_deps_for_winner}
		multiply_variable = {ARG_num_of_deps_for_winner = 0.666}
		multiply_variable = {ARG_num_of_deps_for_second = 0.333}
		round_variable = ARG_num_of_deps_for_winner
		round_variable = ARG_num_of_deps_for_second

		#We need to calculate the split between cycle 1 and cycle 2 reps#
		#3 conditions, if either are 0 and if neither are 0#
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {ARG_no_of_cycle_1_deputies = 0}
			}
			set_variable = {ARG_cycle_2_split = 1}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {ARG_no_of_cycle_2_deputies = 0}
			}
			set_variable = {ARG_cycle_1_split = 1}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {ARG_no_of_cycle_1_deputies > 0}
				check_variable = {ARG_no_of_cycle_2_deputies > 0}
			}
			set_variable = {ARG_total_deps_in_this_state = ARG_no_of_cycle_1_deputies}
			add_to_variable = {ARG_total_deps_in_this_state = ARG_no_of_cycle_2_deputies}
			set_variable = {ARG_cycle_1_split = ARG_no_of_cycle_1_deputies}
			set_variable = {ARG_cycle_2_split = ARG_no_of_cycle_2_deputies}
			divide_variable = {ARG_cycle_1_split = ARG_total_deps_in_this_state}
			divide_variable = {ARG_cycle_2_split = ARG_total_deps_in_this_state}
		}

		clear_array = ARG_POL_all_parties_in_state
		for_each_loop = {
			array = ARG.ARG_POL_active_subparties
			index = idx
			value = party_idx

			add_to_array = {ARG_POL_all_parties_in_state = ARG_POL_sub_party_deps_state_change^party_idx}
		}
		find_highest_in_array = { array = ARG_POL_all_parties_in_state }
		set_variable = {ARG_POL_deps_state_prediction_cycle_1^i = ARG_num_of_deps_for_winner}
		set_variable = {ARG_POL_deps_state_prediction_cycle_2^i = ARG_num_of_deps_for_winner}
		multiply_variable = {ARG_POL_deps_state_prediction_cycle_1^i = ARG_cycle_1_split}
		multiply_variable = {ARG_POL_deps_state_prediction_cycle_2^i = ARG_cycle_2_split}
		round_variable = ARG_POL_deps_state_prediction_cycle_1^i
		round_variable = ARG_POL_deps_state_prediction_cycle_2^i
		set_variable = {ARG_deps_total_predicted_for_state_cycle_1 = ARG_POL_deps_state_prediction_cycle_1^i}
		set_variable = {ARG_deps_total_predicted_for_state_cycle_2 = ARG_POL_deps_state_prediction_cycle_2^i}

		set_variable = {ARG_POL_all_parties_in_state^i = 0}

		find_highest_in_array = { array = ARG_POL_all_parties_in_state }
		set_variable = {ARG_POL_deps_state_prediction_cycle_1^i = ARG_num_of_deps_for_second}
		set_variable = {ARG_POL_deps_state_prediction_cycle_2^i = ARG_num_of_deps_for_second}
		multiply_variable = {ARG_POL_deps_state_prediction_cycle_1^i = ARG_cycle_1_split}
		multiply_variable = {ARG_POL_deps_state_prediction_cycle_2^i = ARG_cycle_2_split}
		round_variable = ARG_POL_deps_state_prediction_cycle_1^i
		round_variable = ARG_POL_deps_state_prediction_cycle_2^i
		add_to_variable = {ARG_deps_total_predicted_for_state_cycle_1 = ARG_POL_deps_state_prediction_cycle_1^i}
		add_to_variable = {ARG_deps_total_predicted_for_state_cycle_2 = ARG_POL_deps_state_prediction_cycle_2^i}



		#Finally just need to run a check to make sure no-one has more than they should#
		ARG_POL_check_for_extra_deps_prediction = yes

		#Since this is meant to be a fresh election then we can do set then add#
		for_each_loop = {
			array = ARG.ARG_POL_active_subparties
			index = idx
			value = party_idx

			set_variable = {ARG_POL_deps_state_prediction^party_idx = ARG_POL_deps_state_prediction_cycle_1^party_idx}
			add_to_variable = {ARG_POL_deps_state_prediction^party_idx = ARG_POL_deps_state_prediction_cycle_2^party_idx}
		}
		#set_variable = {ARG_POL_psa_deps_state_prediction = ARG_POL_deps_state_prediction_cycle_1^0}
		#set_variable = {ARG_POL_psd_deps_state_prediction = ARG_POL_deps_state_prediction_cycle_1^1}
#
		#set_variable = {ARG_POL_ucrp_mir_deps_state_prediction = ARG_POL_deps_state_prediction_cycle_1^2}
		#set_variable = {ARG_POL_ucr_u_mu_deps_state_prediction = ARG_POL_deps_state_prediction_cycle_1^3}
		#set_variable = {ARG_POL_ucrp_lc_deps_state_prediction = ARG_POL_deps_state_prediction_cycle_1^4}
		#set_variable = {ARG_POL_ucr_u_mir_deps_state_prediction = ARG_POL_deps_state_prediction_cycle_1^5}
		#set_variable = {ARG_POL_ucr_ip_deps_state_prediction = ARG_POL_deps_state_prediction_cycle_1^6}

ARG_POL_check_for_extra_deps = {
	#cycle 1#
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = {
				check_variable = {ARG_deps_total_elected_for_state_cycle_1 = ARG_no_of_cycle_1_deputies}
			}
		}
		set_variable = {ARG_deps_difference_cycle_1 = ARG_no_of_cycle_1_deputies}
		subtract_from_variable = {ARG_deps_difference_cycle_1 = ARG_deps_total_elected_for_state_cycle_1}
		clear_array = ARG_POL_num_of_cycle_1_deps
		for_each_loop = {
			array = ARG.ARG_POL_active_subparties
			index = idx
			value = party_idx

			add_to_array = {ARG_POL_num_of_cycle_1_deps = ARG_POL_deps_state_cycle_1^party_idx}
		}
		find_highest_in_array = { array = ARG_POL_num_of_cycle_1_deps }
		add_to_variable = {ARG_POL_deps_state_cycle_1^i = ARG_deps_difference_cycle_1}
	}
	#cycle 2#
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = {
				check_variable = {ARG_deps_total_elected_for_state_cycle_2 = ARG_no_of_cycle_2_deputies}
			}
		}
		set_variable = {ARG_deps_difference_cycle_2 = ARG_no_of_cycle_2_deputies}
		subtract_from_variable = {ARG_deps_difference_cycle_2 = ARG_deps_total_elected_for_state_cycle_2}
		clear_array = ARG_POL_num_of_cycle_2_deps
		for_each_loop = {
			array = ARG.ARG_POL_active_subparties
			index = idx
			value = party_idx

			add_to_array = {ARG_POL_num_of_cycle_2_deps = ARG_POL_deps_state_cycle_2^party_idx}
		}
		find_highest_in_array = { array = ARG_POL_num_of_cycle_2_deps }
		add_to_variable = {ARG_POL_deps_state_cycle_2^i = ARG_deps_difference_cycle_2}
	}
}
ARG_POL_check_for_extra_deps_prediction = {
	#cycle 1#
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = {
				check_variable = {ARG_deps_total_predicted_for_state_cycle_1 = ARG_no_of_cycle_1_deputies}
			}
		}
		set_variable = {ARG_deps_difference_cycle_1 = ARG_no_of_cycle_1_deputies}
		subtract_from_variable = {ARG_deps_difference_cycle_1 = ARG_deps_total_predicted_for_state_cycle_1}
		clear_array = ARG_POL_num_of_cycle_1_deps
		for_each_loop = {
			array = ARG.ARG_POL_active_subparties
			index = idx
			value = party_idx

			add_to_array = {ARG_POL_num_of_cycle_1_deps = ARG_POL_deps_state_prediction_cycle_1^party_idx}
		}
		find_highest_in_array = { array = ARG_POL_num_of_cycle_1_deps }
		add_to_variable = {ARG_POL_deps_state_prediction_cycle_1^i = ARG_deps_difference_cycle_1}
	}
	#cycle 2#
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = {
				check_variable = {ARG_deps_total_predicted_for_state_cycle_2 = ARG_no_of_cycle_2_deputies}
			}
		}
		set_variable = {ARG_deps_difference_cycle_2 = ARG_no_of_cycle_2_deputies}
		subtract_from_variable = {ARG_deps_difference_cycle_2 = ARG_deps_total_predicted_for_state_cycle_2}
		clear_array = ARG_POL_num_of_cycle_2_deps
		for_each_loop = {
			array = ARG.ARG_POL_active_subparties
			index = idx
			value = party_idx

			add_to_array = {ARG_POL_num_of_cycle_2_deps = ARG_POL_deps_state_prediction_cycle_2^party_idx}
		}
		find_highest_in_array = { array = ARG_POL_num_of_cycle_2_deps }
		add_to_variable = {ARG_POL_deps_state_prediction_cycle_2^i = ARG_deps_difference_cycle_2}
	}
}
ARG_POL_hold_senate_elections = {
	ARG_POL_save_current_elections_sens_count = yes
	ARG_POL_update_party_pops = yes
	every_owned_state = {
		limit = {
			has_state_flag = ARG_election_state
		}
		clear_variable = senator_election_var
	}
	for_each_loop = {
		array = ARG_POL_active_parties
		index = idx
		value = party_idx

		clear_variable = ARG_number_of_sens^party_idx
		clear_array = party_idx:ARG_senator_locations
	}
	#clear_variable = ARG_number_of_sens^1
	#clear_variable = ARG_number_of_sens^2
	#clear_variable = ARG_number_of_sens^3
	#clear_variable = ARG_number_of_sens^4
	#clear_variable = ARG_number_of_sens^5
	#clear_variable = ARG_number_of_sens^6
	#clear_variable = ARG_number_of_sens^7
	#clear_variable = ARG_number_of_sens^8
	#clear_variable = ARG_number_of_sens^9
	#clear_array = ARG_ps_senator_locations
	#clear_array = ARG_ucrp_senator_locations
	#clear_array = ARG_ucri_senator_locations
	#clear_array = ARG_pdc_senator_locations
	#clear_array = ARG_fnpc_senator_locations
	#clear_array = ARG_np_senator_locations
	#clear_array = ARG_pdp_senator_locations
	#clear_array = ARG_prn_senator_locations
	#clear_array = ARG_other_senator_locations
	#To clarify here if senator_election_var = :
	#1 - Means only 1st Senator is up for election
	#2 - Means only 2nd Senator is up for election
	#3 - Means both senators are up for election
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = cycle_1_sen_election
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				has_state_flag = senator_1_cycle_1
			}
			add_to_variable = {senator_election_var = 1}
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				has_state_flag = senator_2_cycle_1
			}
			add_to_variable = {senator_election_var = 2}
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = cycle_1_sen_election
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				has_state_flag = senator_1_cycle_2
			}
			add_to_variable = {senator_election_var = 1}
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				has_state_flag = senator_2_cycle_2
			}
			add_to_variable = {senator_election_var = 2}
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = cycle_3_sen_election
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				has_state_flag = senator_1_cycle_3
			}
			add_to_variable = {senator_election_var = 1}
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				has_state_flag = senator_2_cycle_3
			}
			add_to_variable = {senator_election_var = 2}
		}
	}
	#Variable set so now all we need to do is decide the senators
	every_owned_state = {
		limit = {
			has_state_flag = ARG_election_state
		}
		ARG_total_up_state_legs = yes
		clear_array = ARG_senator_array
		ARG_POL_determine_state_leg_split = yes
		for_each_loop = {
			array = ARG.ARG_POL_active_parties
			index = idx
			value = party_idx

			add_to_array = {ARG_senator_array = total_percent_votes^party_idx}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {senator_election_var = 1}
			}
			find_highest_in_array = { array = ARG_senator_array }
			set_variable = {ARG_senator_1 = i}
			add_to_variable = {ARG_senator_1 = 1}
			set_variable = {ARG_state_senators_updated = 0}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {senator_election_var = 2}
			}
			find_highest_in_array = { array = ARG_senator_array }
			set_variable = {ARG_senator_2 = i}
			add_to_variable = {ARG_senator_2 = 1}
			set_variable = {ARG_state_senators_updated = 0}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {senator_election_var = 3}
			}
			find_highest_in_array = { array = ARG_senator_array }
			set_variable = {ARG_senator_1 = i}
			add_to_variable = {ARG_senator_1 = 1}
			set_variable = {ARG_state_senators_updated = 0}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						check_variable = {ARG_senator_array^i = 0.5}
						check_variable = {ARG_senator_array^i > 0.5}
					}
				}
				set_variable = {ARG_senator_2 = i}
				add_to_variable = {ARG_senator_2 = 1}
			}
			else = {
				set_variable = {ARG_senator_array^i = 0}
				find_highest_in_array = { array = ARG_senator_array }
				set_variable = {ARG_senator_2 = i}
				add_to_variable = {ARG_senator_2 = 1}
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = {ARG.ARG_number_of_sens^ARG_senator_1 = 1}
		set_variable = {ARG.ARG_senator_1_location^ARG_senator_1 = THIS}
		add_to_variable = {ARG.ARG_number_of_sens^ARG_senator_2 = 1}
		set_variable = {ARG.ARG_senator_2_location^ARG_senator_2 = THIS}

		ARG = {
			ARG_senate_add_to_locations_array = yes
		}
		set_variable = {ARG_senator_2_display = ARG_senator_2}
		add_to_variable = {ARG_senator_2_display = 10}
	}
	for_each_loop = {
		array = ARG.ARG_POL_active_subparties
		index = idx
		value = party_idx

		clear_variable = ARG_num_of_sens_cycle_1^party_idx
		clear_variable = ARG_num_of_sens_cycle_2^party_idx
		clear_variable = ARG_num_of_sens_cycle_3^party_idx
	}
	every_owned_state = {
		limit = {
			has_state_flag = senator_1_cycle_1
		}
		add_to_variable = {ARG.ARG_num_of_sens_cycle_1^ARG_senator_1 = 1}
	}
	every_owned_state = {
		limit = {
			has_state_flag = senator_2_cycle_1
		}
		add_to_variable = {ARG.ARG_num_of_sens_cycle_1^ARG_senator_2 = 1}
	}
	every_owned_state = {
		limit = {
			has_state_flag = senator_1_cycle_2
		}
		add_to_variable = {ARG.ARG_num_of_sens_cycle_2^ARG_senator_1 = 1}
	}
	every_owned_state = {
		limit = {
			has_state_flag = senator_2_cycle_2
		}
		add_to_variable = {ARG.ARG_num_of_sens_cycle_2^ARG_senator_2 = 1}
	}
	every_owned_state = {
		limit = {
			has_state_flag = senator_1_cycle_3
		}
		add_to_variable = {ARG.ARG_num_of_sens_cycle_3^ARG_senator_1 = 1}
	}
	every_owned_state = {
		limit = {
			has_state_flag = senator_2_cycle_3
		}
		add_to_variable = {ARG.ARG_num_of_sens_cycle_3^ARG_senator_2 = 1}
	}

	clear_variable = ARG_senate_tally
	clear_array = ARG_senate_tally_array

	for_each_loop = {
		array = ARG.ARG_POL_active_parties
		index = idx
		value = party_idx

		set_variable = {ARG_senators^party_idx = ARG_number_of_sens^party_idx}

		add_to_array = {ARG_senate_tally_array = ARG_senate_tally}
		add_to_variable = {ARG_senate_tally = ARG_number_of_sens^party_idx}
	}
	for_each_loop = {
		array = ARG.senate_political_parties
		index = idx
		value = party_idx

		set_variable = {ARG_number_of_senators_display^idx = ARG_senate_tally_array^idx}
		multiply_variable = {ARG_number_of_senators_display^idx = 100}
		add_to_variable = {ARG_number_of_senators_display^idx = ARG_number_of_sens^party_idx}
		multiply_variable = {ARG_number_of_senators_display^idx = 10}
		add_to_variable = {ARG_number_of_senators_display^idx = party_idx}
	}
	#set_variable = {PS_senators = ARG_number_of_sens^1}
	#set_variable = {UCRP_senators = ARG_number_of_sens^2}
	#set_variable = {UCRI_senators = ARG_number_of_sens^3}
	#set_variable = {PDC_senators = ARG_number_of_sens^4}
	#set_variable = {FNPC_senators = ARG_number_of_sens^5}
	#set_variable = {NP_senators = ARG_number_of_sens^6}
	#set_variable = {PDP_senators = ARG_number_of_sens^7}
	#set_variable = {PRN_senators = ARG_number_of_sens^8}
	#set_variable = {OTHER_senators = ARG_number_of_sens^9}
	#for_loop_effect = {
	#	start = 0
	#	end = 9
	#	value = idx
#
	#	add_to_array = {ARG_senate_tally_array = ARG_senate_tally}
	#	add_to_variable = {ARG_senate_tally = ARG_number_of_sens^idx}
	#}
	#for_loop_effect = {
	#	start = 0
	#	end = 9
	#	value = idx
#
	#	set_variable = {ARG_POL_party_senate = senate_political_parties^idx}
	#	set_variable = {ARG_number_of_senators_display^idx = ARG_senate_tally_array^ARG_POL_party_senate}
	#	multiply_variable = {ARG_number_of_senators_display^idx = 100}
	#	add_to_variable = {ARG_number_of_senators_display^idx = ARG_number_of_sens^ARG_POL_party_senate}
	#	multiply_variable = {ARG_number_of_senators_display^idx = 10}
	#	add_to_variable = {ARG_number_of_senators_display^idx = ARG_POL_party_senate}
	#}

	ARG_POL_sortout_senate = yes
	ARG_POL_display_senate_election_results_change = yes
}
ARG_POL_predict_senate_elections = {
	ARG_POL_update_party_pops = yes

	ARG_POL_randomise_pops_for_polls = yes

	every_owned_state = {
		limit = {
			has_state_flag = ARG_election_state
		}
		clear_variable = senator_election_var
	}
	for_each_loop = {
		array = ARG.ARG_POL_active_parties
		index = idx
		value = party_idx

		clear_variable = ARG_number_of_sens_prediction^party_idx
	}
	#clear_variable = ARG_number_of_sens_prediction^1
	#clear_variable = ARG_number_of_sens_prediction^2
	#clear_variable = ARG_number_of_sens_prediction^3
	#clear_variable = ARG_number_of_sens_prediction^4
	#clear_variable = ARG_number_of_sens_prediction^5
	#clear_variable = ARG_number_of_sens_prediction^6
	#clear_variable = ARG_number_of_sens_prediction^7
	#clear_variable = ARG_number_of_sens_prediction^8
	#clear_variable = ARG_number_of_sens_prediction^9
	#To clarify here if senator_election_var = :
	#1 - Means only 1st Senator is up for election
	#2 - Means only 2nd Senator is up for election
	#3 - Means both senators are up for election
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = cycle_1_sen_election
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				has_state_flag = senator_1_cycle_1
			}
			add_to_variable = {senator_election_var = 1}
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				has_state_flag = senator_2_cycle_1
			}
			add_to_variable = {senator_election_var = 2}
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = cycle_1_sen_election
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				has_state_flag = senator_1_cycle_2
			}
			add_to_variable = {senator_election_var = 1}
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				has_state_flag = senator_2_cycle_2
			}
			add_to_variable = {senator_election_var = 2}
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = cycle_3_sen_election
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				has_state_flag = senator_1_cycle_3
			}
			add_to_variable = {senator_election_var = 1}
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				has_state_flag = senator_2_cycle_3
			}
			add_to_variable = {senator_election_var = 2}
		}
	}
	#Variable set so now all we need to do is decide the senators
	every_owned_state = {
		limit = {
			has_state_flag = ARG_election_state
		}
		clear_array = ARG_senator_array
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_state_flag = state_legislature_election
			}
			ARG_total_up_state_legs_prediction = yes
			for_each_loop = {
				array = ARG.ARG_POL_active_parties
				index = idx
				value = party_idx

				set_variable = {ARG_total_deps_state_leg_to_use^party_idx = ARG_total_deps_in_state_leg_prediction^party_idx}
				set_variable = {ARG_total_sens_state_leg_to_use^party_idx = ARG_total_sens_in_state_leg_prediction^party_idx}
			}
		}
		else = {
			ARG_total_up_state_legs = yes
			for_each_loop = {
				array = ARG.ARG_POL_active_parties
				index = idx
				value = party_idx

				set_variable = {ARG_total_deps_state_leg_to_use^party_idx = ARG_total_deps_in_state_leg^party_idx}
				set_variable = {ARG_total_sens_state_leg_to_use^party_idx = ARG_total_sens_in_state_leg^party_idx}
			}
		}
		for_each_loop = {
			array = ARG.ARG_POL_active_parties
			index = idx
			value = party_idx

			set_variable = {total_percent_votes^party_idx = ARG_total_deps_state_leg_to_use^party_idx}
			divide_variable = {total_percent_votes^party_idx = ARG_state_deputies}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {ARG_state_legislatures > 0}
			}
			for_each_loop = {
				array = ARG.ARG_POL_active_parties
				index = idx
				value = party_idx

				set_variable = {sens_percent_votes^party_idx = ARG_total_sens_state_leg_to_use^party_idx}
				divide_variable = {sens_percent_votes^party_idx = ARG_state_legislatures}
				add_to_variable = {total_percent_votes^party_idx = sens_percent_votes^party_idx}
				divide_variable = {total_percent_votes^party_idx = 2} #Take an average
			}
		}
		for_each_loop = {
			array = ARG.ARG_POL_active_parties
			index = idx
			value = party_idx

			add_to_array = {ARG_senator_array = total_percent_votes^party_idx}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {senator_election_var = 1}
			}
			find_highest_in_array = { array = ARG_senator_array }
			set_variable = {ARG_senator_1_prediction = i}
			add_to_variable = {ARG_senator_1_prediction = 1}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {senator_election_var = 2}
			}
			find_highest_in_array = { array = ARG_senator_array }
			set_variable = {ARG_senator_2_prediction = i}
			add_to_variable = {ARG_senator_2_prediction = 1}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {senator_election_var = 3}
			}
			find_highest_in_array = { array = ARG_senator_array }
			set_variable = {ARG_senator_1_prediction = i}
			add_to_variable = {ARG_senator_1_prediction = 1}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						check_variable = {ARG_senator_array^i = 0.5}
						check_variable = {ARG_senator_array^i > 0.5}
					}
				}
				set_variable = {ARG_senator_2_prediction = i}
				add_to_variable = {ARG_senator_2_prediction = 1}
			}
			else = {
				set_variable = {ARG_senator_array^i = 0}
				find_highest_in_array = { array = ARG_senator_array }
				set_variable = {ARG_senator_2_prediction = i}
				add_to_variable = {ARG_senator_2_prediction = 1}
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = {ARG.ARG_number_of_sens_prediction^ARG_senator_1_prediction = 1}
		add_to_variable = {ARG.ARG_number_of_sens_prediction^ARG_senator_2_prediction = 1}
	}
	for_each_loop = {
		array = ARG.ARG_POL_active_parties
		index = idx
		value = party_idx

		clear_variable = ARG_num_of_sens_cycle_1^party_idx
		clear_variable = ARG_num_of_sens_cycle_2^party_idx
		clear_variable = ARG_num_of_sens_cycle_3^party_idx
	}
	every_owned_state = {
		limit = {
			has_state_flag = senator_1_cycle_1
		}
		add_to_variable = {ARG.ARG_num_of_sens_cycle_1_prediction^ARG_senator_1_prediction = 1}
	}
	every_owned_state = {
		limit = {
			has_state_flag = senator_2_cycle_1
		}
		add_to_variable = {ARG.ARG_num_of_sens_cycle_1_prediction^ARG_senator_2_prediction = 1}
	}
	every_owned_state = {
		limit = {
			has_state_flag = senator_1_cycle_2
		}
		add_to_variable = {ARG.ARG_num_of_sens_cycle_2_prediction^ARG_senator_1_prediction = 1}
	}
	every_owned_state = {
		limit = {
			has_state_flag = senator_2_cycle_2
		}
		add_to_variable = {ARG.ARG_num_of_sens_cycle_2_prediction^ARG_senator_2_prediction = 1}
	}
	every_owned_state = {
		limit = {
			has_state_flag = senator_1_cycle_3
		}
		add_to_variable = {ARG.ARG_num_of_sens_cycle_3_prediction^ARG_senator_1_prediction = 1}
	}
	every_owned_state = {
		limit = {
			has_state_flag = senator_2_cycle_3
		}
		add_to_variable = {ARG.ARG_num_of_sens_cycle_3_prediction^ARG_senator_2_prediction = 1}
	}
	for_each_loop = {
		array = ARG.ARG_POL_active_parties
		index = idx
		value = party_idx

		set_variable = {ARG_number_of_sens_predicted_change^party_idx = ARG_number_of_sens_prediction^party_idx}
		subtract_from_variable = {ARG_number_of_sens_predicted_change^party_idx = ARG_number_of_sens^party_idx}
	}

	ARG_sort_out_list_of_parties_senate_seats_prediction = yes
}
ARG_POL_tally_up_sens = {
	clear_variable = ARG_sens_rolling_tally
	for_each_loop = {
		array = ARG.ARG_POL_active_parties
		index = idx
		value = party_idx

		add_to_variable = {ARG_sens_rolling_tally = ARG_num_of_sens_cycle_1^party_idx}
		set_variable = {ARG_POL_sens_end_point_cycle_1^party_idx = ARG_sens_rolling_tally}

		add_to_variable = {ARG_sens_rolling_tally = ARG_num_of_sens_cycle_2^party_idx}
		set_variable = {ARG_POL_sens_end_point_cycle_2^party_idx = ARG_sens_rolling_tally}

		add_to_variable = {ARG_sens_rolling_tally = ARG_num_of_sens_cycle_3^party_idx}
		set_variable = {ARG_POL_sens_end_point_cycle_3^party_idx = ARG_sens_rolling_tally}
	}
}

		}
		set_variable = {ARG_previous_point = ARG_POL_sens_end_point_cycle_3^party_idx}
	}

ARG_POL_highlight_cycle_3_sens = {
	ARG_POL_tally_up_sens = yes

	clear_variable = ARG_previous_point
	for_each_loop = {
		array = ARG.ARG_POL_active_parties
		index = idx
		value = party_idx

		set_variable = {ARG_previous_point = ARG_POL_sens_end_point_cycle_2^party_idx}

			end = ARG_POL_sens_end_point_cycle_3^party_idx

	#for_loop_effect = {

#

ARG_POL_sortout_senate = {
	clear_variable = ARG_previous_startpoint
	clear_variable = ARG_POL_senate_tally_var
	for_each_loop = {
		array = ARG.ARG_POL_active_parties
		index = idx
		value = party_idx

		set_variable = {ARG_startpoint_senate^party_idx = ARG_previous_startpoint}
		add_to_variable = {ARG_startpoint_senate^party_idx = ARG_senators^party_idx}

		ARG_POL_GUI_combine_locations_array = yes

		for_loop_effect = {
			start = ARG_previous_startpoint
			end = ARG_startpoint_senate^party_idx
			value = jdx

			set_variable = { ARG_frame_senate_array^jdx = party_idx }

			add_to_variable = {ARG_POL_senate_tally_var = 1}
			set_variable = {ARG_frame_senate_array_display^jdx = ARG_POL_senate_tally_var}
			multiply_variable = {ARG_frame_senate_array_display^jdx = 1000}
			add_to_variable = {ARG_frame_senate_array_display^jdx = 48}
			multiply_variable = {ARG_frame_senate_array_display^jdx = 10}
			add_to_variable = {ARG_frame_senate_array_display^jdx = ARG_frame_senate_array^jdx}
		}

		set_variable = {ARG_previous_startpoint = ARG_startpoint_senate^party_idx}
	}
