ARG_sort_out_list_of_parties_senate_seats = {
	clear_array = senate_political_parties
	for_each_loop = {
		array = ARG.ARG_POL_active_parties
		index = idx
		value = party_idx

		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {ARG_number_of_sens^party_idx > 0}
			}
			add_to_array = { senate_political_parties = party_idx }
		}
	}
}
ARG_sort_out_list_of_parties_senate_seats_prediction = {
	clear_array = senate_political_parties
	for_each_loop = {
		array = ARG.ARG_POL_active_parties
		index = idx
		value = party_idx

		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					NOT = {
						check_variable = {ARG_number_of_sens_predicted_change^party_idx = 0}
					}
					check_variable = {ARG_number_of_sens^party_idx > 0}
				}
			}
			add_to_array = { senate_political_parties = party_idx }
		}
	}
}
ARG_state_legislature_elections = { #Good news, the state legislature is completly redone when elected so it makes it a lot more easy
	ARG_POL_update_party_pops = yes
	every_owned_state = {
		limit = {
			has_state_flag = ARG_election_state
			has_state_flag = state_legislature_election
		}
		ARG_POL_save_current_elections_state_legs_count = yes
		clear_variable = ARG_total_state_leg_deps #This is a suprise tool that'll help us out later
		#First up the congress, as every state has that#
		for_each_loop = {
			array = ARG.ARG_POL_active_parties
			index = idx
			value = party_idx

			multiply_variable = {ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^party_idx = ARG_state_deputies}
			round_variable = ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^party_idx
			#And now we check for the inconsistencies#
			add_to_variable = {ARG_total_state_leg_deps = ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^party_idx} #See I told you
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					check_variable = {ARG_total_state_leg_deps = ARG_state_deputies}
				}
			}
			set_variable = {state_leg_difference_deps = ARG_state_deputies}
			subtract_from_variable = {state_leg_difference_deps = ARG_total_state_leg_deps}
			clear_array = ARG_state_legs_deps_array
			for_each_loop = {
				array = ARG.ARG_POL_active_parties
				index = idx
				value = party_idx

				add_to_array = {ARG_state_legs_deps_array = ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^party_idx}
			}
			find_highest_in_array = { array = ARG_state_legs_deps_array }
			add_to_variable = {ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^i = state_leg_difference_deps}
		}
		set_state_flag = distribute_state_leg_deps
		set_variable = {ARG_state_congress_update = 1}
		ARG_POL_distribute_state_leg = yes
		#Now we do the senate, basically the same, but some don't have one
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {ARG_state_legislatures > 0}
			}
			ARG = {
				ARG_POL_update_party_pops = yes
			}
			set_variable = {ARG_state_senate_update = 1}
			clear_variable = ARG_total_state_leg_sens #This is a suprise tool that'll help us out later
			#First up the congress, as every state has that#
			for_each_loop = {
				array = ARG.ARG_POL_active_parties
				index = idx
				value = party_idx

				multiply_variable = {ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^party_idx = ARG_state_legislatures}
				round_variable = ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^party_idx
				#And now we check for the inconsistencies#
				add_to_variable = {ARG_total_state_leg_sens = ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^party_idx} #See I told you
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						check_variable = {ARG_total_state_leg_sens = ARG_state_legislatures}
					}
				}
				set_variable = {state_leg_difference_sens = ARG_state_legislatures}
				subtract_from_variable = {state_leg_difference_sens = ARG_total_state_leg_sens}
				clear_array = ARG_state_legs_sens_array
				for_each_loop = {
					array = ARG.ARG_POL_active_parties
					index = idx
					value = party_idx

					add_to_array = {ARG_state_legs_sens_array = ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^party_idx}
				}
				find_highest_in_array = { array = ARG_state_legs_sens_array }
				add_to_variable = {ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^i = state_leg_difference_sens}
			}
			set_state_flag = distribute_state_leg_sens
			ARG_POL_distribute_state_leg = yes
		}
		#Finally just gotta do govenors
		ARG_total_up_state_legs = yes
		for_each_loop = {
			array = ARG.ARG_POL_active_parties
			index = idx
			value = party_idx

			set_variable = {total_percent_votes^party_idx = ARG_total_deps_in_state_leg^party_idx}
			divide_variable = {total_percent_votes^party_idx = ARG_state_deputies}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {ARG_state_legislatures > 0}
			}
			for_each_loop = {
				array = ARG.ARG_POL_active_parties
				index = idx
				value = party_idx

				set_variable = {sens_percent_votes^party_idx = ARG_total_sens_in_state_leg^party_idx}
				divide_variable = {sens_percent_votes^party_idx = ARG_state_legislatures}
				add_to_variable = {total_percent_votes^party_idx = sens_percent_votes^party_idx}
				divide_variable = {total_percent_votes^party_idx = 2} #Take an average
			}
		}
		clear_array = ARG_state_govenor_array
		for_each_loop = {
			array = ARG.ARG_POL_active_parties
			index = idx
			value = party_idx

			add_to_array = {ARG_state_govenor_array = total_percent_votes^party_idx}
		}
		find_highest_in_array = {
			array = ARG_state_govenor_array
			index = gov_idx
		}
		set_variable = {ARG_state_govenor = gov_idx}
		add_to_variable = {ARG_state_govenor = 1}
		ARG_POL_setup_governor_tally_vars = yes
		set_variable = {ARG_state_governor_display = ARG_POL_governor_tally_array^gov_idx}
		multiply_variable = {ARG_state_governor_display = 100}
		add_to_variable = {ARG_state_governor_display = ARG_state_deputies}
		multiply_variable = {ARG_state_governor_display = 10}
		add_to_variable = {ARG_state_governor_display = ARG_state_govenor}

		set_variable = {ARG_state_governor_update = 0}
		ARG_POL_calculate_election_change_state_leg = yes

	}
	ARG = {
		ARG_POL_setup_views_for_state_legs = yes
	}
}
ARG_POL_setup_governor_tally_vars = {
	clear_variable = ARG_POL_governor_tally_var
	clear_array = ARG_POL_governor_tally_array
	for_each_loop = {
		array = ARG.ARG_POL_active_parties
		index = idx
		value = party_idx

		add_to_variable = {ARG_POL_governor_tally_var = ARG_total_deps_in_state_leg^party_idx}
		add_to_array = {ARG_POL_governor_tally_array = ARG_POL_governor_tally_var}
	}
}
ARG_state_legislature_election_prediction = { #Good news, the state legislature is completly redone when elected so it makes it a lot more easy
	ARG_POL_update_party_pops = yes
	every_owned_state = {
		limit = {
			has_state_flag = ARG_election_state
			has_state_flag = state_legislature_election
		}
		clear_variable = ARG_total_state_leg_deps #This is a suprise tool that'll help us out later
		#First up the congress, as every state has that#
		for_each_loop = {
			array = ARG.ARG_POL_active_parties
			index = idx
			value = party_idx

			multiply_variable = {ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^party_idx = ARG_state_deputies}
			round_variable = ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^party_idx
			#And now we check for the inconsistencies#
			add_to_variable = {ARG_total_state_leg_deps = ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^party_idx} #See I told you
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					check_variable = {ARG_total_state_leg_deps = ARG_state_deputies}
				}
			}
			set_variable = {state_leg_difference_deps = ARG_state_deputies}
			subtract_from_variable = {state_leg_difference_deps = ARG_total_state_leg_deps}
			clear_array = ARG_state_legs_deps_array
			for_each_loop = {
				array = ARG.ARG_POL_active_parties
				index = idx
				value = party_idx

				add_to_array = {ARG_state_legs_deps_array = ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^party_idx}
			}
			find_highest_in_array = { array = ARG_state_legs_deps_array }
			add_to_variable = {ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^i = state_leg_difference_deps}
		}
		set_state_flag = distribute_state_leg_deps
		ARG_POL_distribute_state_leg_predictions = yes
		#Now we do the senate, basically the same, but some don't have one
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {ARG_state_legislatures > 0}
			}
			ARG = {
				ARG_POL_update_party_pops = yes
			}
			clear_variable = ARG_total_state_leg_sens #This is a suprise tool that'll help us out later
			#First up the congress, as every state has that#
			for_each_loop = {
				array = ARG.ARG_POL_active_parties
				index = idx
				value = party_idx

				multiply_variable = {ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^party_idx = ARG_state_legislatures}
				round_variable = ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^party_idx
				#And now we check for the inconsistencies#
				add_to_variable = {ARG_total_state_leg_sens = ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^party_idx} #See I told you
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						check_variable = {ARG_total_state_leg_sens = ARG_state_legislatures}
					}
				}
				set_variable = {state_leg_difference_sens = ARG_state_legislatures}
				subtract_from_variable = {state_leg_difference_sens = ARG_total_state_leg_sens}
				clear_array = ARG_state_legs_sens_array
				for_each_loop = {
					array = ARG.ARG_POL_active_parties
					index = idx
					value = party_idx

					add_to_array = {ARG_state_legs_sens_array = ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^party_idx}
				}
				find_highest_in_array = { array = ARG_state_legs_sens_array }
				add_to_variable = {ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^i = state_leg_difference_sens}
			}
			set_state_flag = distribute_state_leg_sens
			ARG_POL_distribute_state_leg_predictions = yes
		}
		#Finally just gotta do govenors
		ARG_total_up_state_legs_prediction = yes
		for_each_loop = {
			array = ARG.ARG_POL_active_parties
			index = idx
			value = party_idx

			set_variable = {total_percent_votes^party_idx = ARG_total_deps_in_state_leg_prediction^party_idx}
			divide_variable = {total_percent_votes^party_idx = ARG_state_deputies}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {ARG_state_legislatures > 0}
			}
			for_each_loop = {
				array = ARG.ARG_POL_active_parties
				index = idx
				value = party_idx

				set_variable = {sens_percent_votes^party_idx = ARG_total_sens_in_state_leg_prediction^party_idx}
				divide_variable = {sens_percent_votes^party_idx = ARG_state_legislatures}
				add_to_variable = {total_percent_votes^party_idx = sens_percent_votes^idx}
				divide_variable = {total_percent_votes^party_idx = 2} #Take an average
			}
		}
		clear_array = ARG_state_govenor_array
		for_each_loop = {
			array = ARG.ARG_POL_active_parties
			index = idx
			value = party_idx

			add_to_array = {ARG_state_govenor_array = total_percent_votes^party_idx}
		}
		find_highest_in_array = {
			array = ARG_state_govenor_array
			index = gov_idx
		}
		set_variable = {ARG_state_govenor_prediction = gov_idx}
		add_to_variable = {ARG_state_govenor_prediction = 1}

	clear_variable = ARG_state_leg_distribute_check_var
	for_each_loop = {
		array = ARG.ARG_POL_active_subparties
		index = idx
		value = party_idx

		round_variable = ARG_POL_state_leg_update^party_idx
		add_to_variable = {ARG_state_leg_distribute_check_var = ARG_POL_state_leg_update^party_idx}
	}

	if = {
		limit = {
			has_state_flag = distribute_state_leg_deps
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					check_variable = {ARG_state_leg_distribute_check_var = ARG_state_deputies}
				}
			}
			set_variable = {ARG_state_leg_distribute_difference = ARG_state_deputies}
			subtract_from_variable = {ARG_state_leg_distribute_difference = ARG_state_leg_distribute_check_var}
			clear_array = ARG_state_leg_distribute_array
			for_each_loop = {
				array = ARG.ARG_POL_active_subparties
				index = idx
				value = party_idx

				add_to_array = {ARG_state_leg_distribute_array = ARG_POL_state_leg_update^party_idx}
			}
			find_highest_in_array = {array = ARG_state_leg_distribute_array}
			add_to_variable = {ARG_POL_state_leg_update^i = ARG_state_leg_distribute_difference}
		}
		clear_variable = ARG_POL_predicted_amount_check
		clear_variable = ARG_POL_predicted_difference_check
		for_each_loop = {
			array = ARG.ARG_POL_active_subparties
			index = idx
			value = party_idx

			set_variable = {ARG_POL_state_leg_deps_predicted_amount^party_idx = ARG_POL_state_leg_update^party_idx}
			set_variable = {ARG_POL_state_leg_deps_predicted_change^party_idx = ARG_POL_state_leg_update^party_idx}
			subtract_from_variable = {ARG_POL_state_leg_deps_predicted_change^party_idx = ARG_POL_total_state_leg_deps^party_idx}
			add_to_variable = {ARG_POL_predicted_amount_check = ARG_POL_state_leg_deps_predicted_amount^party_idx}
			add_to_variable = {ARG_POL_predicted_difference_check = ARG_POL_state_leg_deps_predicted_change^party_idx}
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_state_flag = distribute_state_leg_sens
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					check_variable = {ARG_state_leg_distribute_check_var = ARG_state_legislatures}
				}
			}
			set_variable = {ARG_state_leg_distribute_difference = ARG_state_legislatures}
			subtract_from_variable = {ARG_state_leg_distribute_difference = ARG_state_leg_distribute_check_var}
			clear_array = ARG_state_leg_distribute_array
			for_each_loop = {
				array = ARG.ARG_POL_active_subparties
				index = idx
				value = party_idx

				add_to_array = {ARG_state_leg_distribute_array = ARG_POL_state_leg_update^party_idx}
			}
			find_highest_in_array = {array = ARG_state_leg_distribute_array}
			add_to_variable = {ARG_POL_state_leg_update^i = ARG_state_leg_distribute_difference}
		}
		for_each_loop = {
			array = ARG.ARG_POL_active_subparties
			index = idx
			value = party_idx

			set_variable = {ARG_POL_state_leg_sens_predicted_amount^party_idx = ARG_POL_state_leg_update^party_idx}
			set_variable = {ARG_POL_state_leg_sens_predicted_change^party_idx = ARG_POL_state_leg_update^party_idx}
			subtract_from_variable = {ARG_POL_state_leg_sens_predicted_change^party_idx = ARG_POL_total_state_leg_sens^party_idx}
		}
	}
	clr_state_flag = distribute_state_leg_deps
	clr_state_flag = distribute_state_leg_sens
}

ARG_POL_setup_views_for_state_legs = {
	ARG_POL_setup_state_leg_vars = yes
	every_owned_state = {
		limit = {
			has_state_flag = ARG_election_state
			has_state_flag = state_legislature_election
		}
		#Congress#
		clear_variable = ARG_POL_tallying_variable
		clear_variable = ARG_previous_startpoint
		for_each_loop = {
			array = ARG.ARG_POL_active_parties
			index = idx
			value = party_idx

			set_variable = {ARG_startpoint^party_idx = ARG_previous_startpoint}
			add_to_variable = {ARG_startpoint^party_idx = ARG_total_deps_in_state_leg^party_idx}
			for_loop_effect = {
				start = ARG_previous_startpoint
				end = ARG_startpoint^party_idx
				value = jdx

				add_to_variable = {ARG_POL_tallying_variable = 1}
				set_variable = {ARG_POL_GUI_cong_seat_display^jdx = ARG_POL_tallying_variable}
				multiply_variable = {ARG_POL_GUI_cong_seat_display^jdx = 1000}
				add_to_variable = {ARG_POL_GUI_cong_seat_display^jdx = ARG_state_deputies}
				add_to_variable = {ARG_POL_GUI_cong_seat_display^jdx = 2}
				multiply_variable = {ARG_POL_GUI_cong_seat_display^jdx = 10}
				add_to_variable = {ARG_POL_GUI_cong_seat_display^jdx = party_idx}
				set_variable = { ARG_POL_GUI_cong_seat^jdx = party_idx }
			}
			set_variable = {ARG_previous_startpoint = ARG_startpoint^party_idx}
		}

ARG_POL_setup_map_effect = {
	ARG_POL_update_party_pops = yes
	every_owned_state = {
		limit = {
			has_state_flag = ARG_election_state
		}
		#Finding the highest#
		clear_array = ARG_state_party_pops_in_order
		for_each_loop = {
			array = ARG.ARG_POL_active_parties
			index = idx
			value = party_idx

			add_to_array = {ARG_state_party_pops_in_order = ARG_POL_party_pop_percent^party_idx}
		}
		find_highest_in_array = { array = ARG_state_party_pops_in_order }
		set_variable = {ARG_first_party = i}
		set_variable = {ARG_first_party_percent = ARG_state_party_pops_in_order^i}
		add_to_variable = {ARG_first_party = 1}

		#Finding the second highest#
		set_variable = {ARG_state_party_pops_in_order^i = 0}
		find_highest_in_array = { array = ARG_state_party_pops_in_order }
		set_variable = {ARG_second_party = i}
		set_variable = {ARG_map_split = ARG_state_party_pops_in_order^ARG_second_party}
		divide_variable = {ARG_map_split = ARG_first_party_percent}
		multiply_variable = {ARG_map_split = 50}
		round_variable = ARG_map_split
		add_to_variable = {ARG_second_party = 1}
		ARG_GUI_combine_map_variable = yes
		ARG_GUI_display_pops_in_order = yes
	}
}
ARG_GUI_combine_map_variable = {
	set_variable = {Arg_map_var = ARG_first_party}
	multiply_variable = {Arg_map_var = 10}
	add_to_variable = {Arg_map_var = ARG_second_party}
	multiply_variable = {Arg_map_var = 1000}
	add_to_variable = {Arg_map_var = ARG_map_split}
}
ARG_GUI_display_pops_in_order = {
	clear_array = ARG_POL_pop_for_state_in_order
	clear_array = ARG_POL_pop_for_state_in_order_index
	clear_array = ARG_POL_pop_for_state
	clear_variable = ARG_POL_pops_total
	clear_array = ARG_POL_GUI_state_pop_for_display_convenience
	for_each_loop = {
		array = ARG.ARG_POL_active_parties
		index = idx
		value = party_idx

		add_to_array = {ARG_POL_pop_for_state = ARG_pol_party_pop^party_idx}
		add_to_variable = {ARG_POL_pops_total = ARG_pol_party_pop^party_idx}
	}
	for_each_loop = {
		array = ARG.ARG_POL_active_parties
		index = idx
		value = party_idx

		divide_variable = {ARG_POL_pop_for_state^idx = ARG_POL_pops_total}
		multiply_variable = {ARG_POL_pop_for_state^idx = 100}
		set_variable = {ARG_POL_GUI_state_pop_for_display_convenience^party_idx = ARG_POL_pop_for_state^idx}
	}
	for_each_loop = {
		array = ARG.ARG_POL_active_parties
		index = idx
		value = party_idx

		find_highest_in_array = {array = ARG_POL_pop_for_state index = jdx}
		add_to_array = {ARG_POL_pop_for_state_in_order = ARG_POL_pop_for_state^jdx}
		set_variable = {ARG_POL_pop_for_state^jdx = 0}
		add_to_array = {ARG_POL_pop_for_state_in_order_index = jdx}
		add_to_variable = {ARG_POL_pop_for_state_in_order_index^idx = 1}
	}
}
ARG_POL_glow_effect_setup = {
	#Parliament#
	clear_array = ARG_x_array_congress_glow
	clear_array = ARG_y_array_congress_glow
	for_loop_effect = {
		start = 0
		end = 192
		value = idx

		set_variable = {x_pos_glow = ARG_x_array_congress^idx}
		set_variable = {y_pos_glow = ARG_y_array_congress^idx}
		subtract_from_variable = {x_pos_glow = 6}
		subtract_from_variable = {y_pos_glow = 6}
		add_to_array = {ARG_x_array_congress_glow = x_pos_glow}
		add_to_array = {ARG_y_array_congress_glow = y_pos_glow}
	}

	clear_array = ARG_x_array_state_glow
	clear_array = ARG_y_array_state_glow
	for_loop_effect = {
		start = 0
		end = 23
		value = idx

		set_variable = {x_pos_glow = ARG_x_array_state^idx}
		set_variable = {y_pos_glow = ARG_y_array_state^idx}
		subtract_from_variable = {x_pos_glow = 3}
		subtract_from_variable = {y_pos_glow = 2}
		add_to_array = {ARG_x_array_state_glow = x_pos_glow}
		add_to_array = {ARG_y_array_state_glow = y_pos_glow}
	}
	#Senate#
	clear_array = ARG_x_array_senate_glow
	clear_array = ARG_y_array_senate_glow
	for_loop_effect = {
		start = 0
		end = 46
		value = idx

		set_variable = {x_pos_glow = ARG_senate_election_array_x^idx}
		set_variable = {y_pos_glow = ARG_senate_election_array_y^idx}
		subtract_from_variable = {x_pos_glow = 6}
		subtract_from_variable = {y_pos_glow = 6}
		add_to_array = {ARG_x_array_senate_glow = x_pos_glow}
		add_to_array = {ARG_y_array_senate_glow = y_pos_glow}
	}
}
ARG_POL_GUI_highlight_all_cycle_1_deps = {
	ARG_POL_GUI_highlight_deps_cycle_1 = yes
	every_owned_state = {
		limit = { has_state_flag = ARG_election_state }
		for_each_loop = {
			array = ARG.ARG_POL_active_subparties
			index = idx
			value = party_idx

			set_variable = {ARG_POL_num_of_cycle_1_deps^party_idx = ARG_POL_deps_state_cycle_1^party_idx}
			set_variable = {ARG_POL_total_num_of_deps^party_idx = ARG_POL_total_deps_in_state^party_idx}
		}
		ARG_POL_GUI_highlight_deps_cycle_1 = yes
	}
}

ARG_POL_GUI_highlight_deps_cycle_2 = {
	#On the parliament display#
	clear_variable = ARG_GUI_sub_parties_rolling_tally
	clear_variable = ARG_previous_startpoint
	for_each_loop = {
		array = ARG.ARG_POL_active_subparties
		index = idx
		value = party_idx

		set_variable = {ARG_POL_highlight_endpoint_cycle_2^idx = ARG_GUI_sub_parties_rolling_tally}
		add_to_variable = {ARG_POL_highlight_endpoint_cycle_2^idx = ARG_POL_num_of_cycle_2_deps^idx}

		add_to_variable = {ARG_GUI_sub_parties_rolling_tally = ARG_POL_total_num_of_deps^party_idx}
		set_variable = {ARG_GUI_sub_parties_end_point^party_idx = ARG_GUI_sub_parties_rolling_tally}

		for_loop_effect = {
			start = ARG_previous_startpoint
			end = ARG_POL_highlight_endpoint_cycle_2^party_idx
			value = jdx

			set_variable = { ARG_POL_GUI_dep_seat_glow^jdx = 1 }
		}
		set_variable = {ARG_previous_startpoint = ARG_GUI_sub_parties_end_point^party_idx}
	}

ARG_POL_GUI_highlight_all_cycle_1_sens = {
	clear_variable = ARG_previous_sens
	clear_variable = ARG_previous_startpoint
	for_each_loop = {
		array = ARG.ARG_POL_active_subparties
		index = idx
		value = party_idx


		set_variable = {ARG_sens_highlight_startpoint^party_idx = ARG_previous_startpoint}
		add_to_variable = {ARG_sens_highlight_startpoint^party_idx = ARG_previous_sens}
		set_variable = {ARG_sens_highlight_endpoint^party_idx = ARG_sens_highlight_startpoint^party_idx}
		add_to_variable = {ARG_sens_highlight_endpoint^party_idx = ARG_num_of_sens_cycle_1^party_idx}

		for_loop_effect = {
			start = ARG_sens_highlight_startpoint^party_idx
			end = ARG_sens_highlight_endpoint^party_idx
			value = jdx

			set_variable = {ARG_senate_highlight^jdx = 1}
		}

		set_variable = {ARG_previous_sens = ARG_number_of_sens^party_idx}
		set_variable = {ARG_previous_startpoint = ARG_sens_highlight_endpoint^party_idx}
	}
	#for_loop_effect = {
	#	start = 1
	#	end = 10
	#	value = idx
#
	#	set_variable = {ARG_prev_index = idx}
	#	subtract_from_variable = {ARG_prev_index = 1}
	#	set_variable = {ARG_sens_highlight_startpoint^idx = ARG_sens_highlight_endpoint^ARG_prev_index}
	#	add_to_variable = {ARG_sens_highlight_startpoint^idx = ARG_number_of_sens^ARG_prev_index}
	#	set_variable = {ARG_sens_highlight_endpoint^idx = ARG_sens_highlight_startpoint^idx}
	#	add_to_variable = {ARG_sens_highlight_endpoint^idx = ARG_num_of_sens_cycle_1^idx}
	#}
#
	#for_loop_effect = {
	#	start = ARG_sens_highlight_startpoint^1
	#	end = ARG_sens_highlight_endpoint^1
	#	value = idx
#
	#	set_variable = {ARG_senate_highlight^idx = 1}
	#}
	#for_loop_effect = {
	#	start = ARG_sens_highlight_startpoint^2
	#	end = ARG_sens_highlight_endpoint^2
	#	value = idx
#
	#	set_variable = {ARG_senate_highlight^idx = 1}
	#}
	#for_loop_effect = {
	#	start = ARG_sens_highlight_startpoint^3
	#	end = ARG_sens_highlight_endpoint^3
	#	value = idx
#
	#	set_variable = {ARG_senate_highlight^idx = 1}
	#}
	#for_loop_effect = {
	#	start = ARG_sens_highlight_startpoint^4
	#	end = ARG_sens_highlight_endpoint^4

	#	set_variable = {ARG_senate_highlight^idx = 1}

	#	end = ARG_sens_highlight_endpoint^6

	#for_loop_effect = {

	#for_loop_effect = {

	#	end = ARG_sens_highlight_endpoint^9
	#	value = idx
#
	#	set_variable = {ARG_senate_highlight^idx = 1}
	#}
	every_owned_state = {
		limit = {
			has_state_flag = ARG_election_state
			has_state_flag = senator_1_cycle_1
		}
		set_variable = {ARG_POL_GUI_senator_1_highlight = 1}
	}
	every_owned_state = {
		limit = {
			has_state_flag = ARG_election_state
			has_state_flag = senator_2_cycle_1
		}
		set_variable = {ARG_POL_GUI_senator_1_highlight = 1}
	}
}
ARG_POL_GUI_highlight_all_cycle_2_sens = {
	clear_variable = ARG_previous_sens
	clear_variable = ARG_previous_startpoint
	for_each_loop = {
		array = ARG.ARG_POL_active_subparties
		index = idx
		value = party_idx


		set_variable = {ARG_sens_highlight_startpoint^party_idx = ARG_previous_startpoint}
		add_to_variable = {ARG_sens_highlight_startpoint^party_idx = ARG_previous_sens}
		add_to_variable = {ARG_sens_highlight_startpoint^party_idx = ARG_num_of_sens_cycle_1^party_idx}
		set_variable = {ARG_sens_highlight_endpoint^party_idx = ARG_sens_highlight_startpoint^party_idx}
		add_to_variable = {ARG_sens_highlight_endpoint^party_idx = ARG_num_of_sens_cycle_2^party_idx}

		for_loop_effect = {
			start = ARG_sens_highlight_startpoint^party_idx
			end = ARG_sens_highlight_endpoint^party_idx
			value = jdx

			set_variable = {ARG_senate_highlight^jdx = 1}
		}

		set_variable = {ARG_previous_sens = ARG_num_of_sens_cycle_3^party_idx}
		set_variable = {ARG_previous_startpoint = ARG_sens_highlight_endpoint^party_idx}
	}

ARG_POL_GUI_highlight_all_cycle_3_sens = {
	clear_variable = ARG_previous_sens
	clear_variable = ARG_previous_startpoint
	for_each_loop = {
		array = ARG.ARG_POL_active_subparties
		index = idx
		value = party_idx


		set_variable = {ARG_sens_highlight_startpoint^party_idx = ARG_previous_startpoint}
		add_to_variable = {ARG_sens_highlight_startpoint^party_idx = ARG_previous_sens}
		set_variable = {ARG_sens_highlight_endpoint^party_idx = ARG_sens_highlight_startpoint^party_idx}
		add_to_variable = {ARG_sens_highlight_endpoint^party_idx = ARG_num_of_sens_cycle_3^party_idx}

		for_loop_effect = {
			start = ARG_sens_highlight_startpoint^party_idx
			end = ARG_sens_highlight_endpoint^party_idx
			value = jdx

			set_variable = {ARG_senate_highlight^jdx = 1}
		}

		set_variable = {ARG_previous_sens = ARG_number_of_sens^party_idx}
		set_variable = {ARG_previous_startpoint = ARG_sens_highlight_endpoint^party_idx}
	}

ARG_POL_GUI_set_all_seat_subparty = {
	ARG_GUI_set_dots_subparty = yes
	every_owned_state = {
		limit = { has_state_flag = ARG_election_state }
		for_each_loop = {
			array = ARG.ARG_POL_active_subparties
			index = idx
			value = party_idx

			set_variable = {ARG_POL_total_num_of_deps^party_idx = ARG_POL_total_deps_in_state^party_idx}
		}
		ARG_GUI_set_dots_subparty = yes
	}
	every_owned_state = {
		limit = { has_state_flag = ARG_election_state }
		ARG_GUI_set_dots_subparty_state_leg = yes
	}
}

ARG_GUI_set_dots_subparty = {
	clear_variable = ARG_GUI_POL_rolling_tally_nation
	clear_variable = ARG_previous_breakpoint
	for_each_loop = {
		array = ARG.ARG_POL_active_subparties
		index = idx
		value = party_idx

		set_variable = {ARG_POL_dep_endpoint^party_idx = ARG_POL_total_num_of_deps^party_idx}
		add_to_variable = {ARG_GUI_POL_rolling_tally_nation = ARG_POL_total_num_of_deps^party_idx}
		set_variable = {ARG_GUI_sub_parties_break_point^party_idx = ARG_GUI_POL_rolling_tally_nation}

		for_loop_effect = {
			start = ARG_previous_breakpoint
			end = ARG_GUI_sub_parties_break_point^party_idx
			value = jdx

			set_variable = { ARG_POL_GUI_dep_seat_subparty^jdx = party_idx }
		}
		set_variable = {ARG_previous_breakpoint = ARG_GUI_sub_parties_break_point^party_idx}
	}

ARG_POL_GUI_clear_highlighted_dots = {
	for_loop_effect = {
		start = 0
		end = 192
		value = idx

		set_variable = { ARG_POL_GUI_dep_seat_glow^idx = 0 }
	}
	for_loop_effect = {
		start = 0
		end = 46
		value = idx

		set_variable = { ARG_senate_highlight^idx = 0 }
	}
	every_owned_state = {
		limit = {
			has_state_flag = ARG_election_state
		}
		for_loop_effect = {
			start = 0
			end = 192
			value = idx

			set_variable = { ARG_POL_GUI_dep_seat_glow^idx = 0 }
		}
		clear_variable = ARG_POL_GUI_senator_1_highlight
		clear_variable = ARG_POL_GUI_senator_2_highlight
		clear_variable = ARG_POL_GUI_state_leg_highlight
	}
}

		set_variable = {ARG_POL_deps_state_cycle_1^3 = 2}

ARG_POL_GUI_display_starting_results = {
	every_owned_state = {
		limit = {
			has_state_flag = ARG_election_state
		}
		ARG_POL_set_vars_startup = yes
	}
	for_each_loop = {
		array = ARG.ARG_POL_active_parties
		index = idx
		value = party_idx

		clear_variable = ARG_num_of_sens_cycle_1^party_idx
		clear_variable = ARG_num_of_sens_cycle_2^party_idx
		clear_variable = ARG_num_of_sens_cycle_3^party_idx
		clear_variable = ARG_number_of_sens^party_idx
	}
	#clear_variable = ARG_num_of_sens_cycle_1^1
	#clear_variable = ARG_num_of_sens_cycle_1^2
	#clear_variable = ARG_num_of_sens_cycle_1^3
	#clear_variable = ARG_num_of_sens_cycle_1^4
	#clear_variable = ARG_num_of_sens_cycle_1^5
	#clear_variable = ARG_num_of_sens_cycle_1^6
	#clear_variable = ARG_num_of_sens_cycle_1^7
	#clear_variable = ARG_num_of_sens_cycle_1^8
	#clear_variable = ARG_num_of_sens_cycle_1^9
#
	#clear_variable = ARG_num_of_sens_cycle_2^1
	#clear_variable = ARG_num_of_sens_cycle_2^2
	#clear_variable = ARG_num_of_sens_cycle_2^3
	#clear_variable = ARG_num_of_sens_cycle_2^4
	#clear_variable = ARG_num_of_sens_cycle_2^5
	#clear_variable = ARG_num_of_sens_cycle_2^6
	#clear_variable = ARG_num_of_sens_cycle_2^7
	#clear_variable = ARG_num_of_sens_cycle_2^8
	#clear_variable = ARG_num_of_sens_cycle_2^9
#
	#clear_variable = ARG_num_of_sens_cycle_3^1
	#clear_variable = ARG_num_of_sens_cycle_3^2
	#clear_variable = ARG_num_of_sens_cycle_3^3
	#clear_variable = ARG_num_of_sens_cycle_3^4
	#clear_variable = ARG_num_of_sens_cycle_3^5
	#clear_variable = ARG_num_of_sens_cycle_3^6
	#clear_variable = ARG_num_of_sens_cycle_3^7
	#clear_variable = ARG_num_of_sens_cycle_3^8
	#clear_variable = ARG_num_of_sens_cycle_3^9
#
	#clear_variable = ARG_number_of_sens^1
	#clear_variable = ARG_number_of_sens^2
	#clear_variable = ARG_number_of_sens^3
	#clear_variable = ARG_number_of_sens^4
	#clear_variable = ARG_number_of_sens^5
	#clear_variable = ARG_number_of_sens^6
	#clear_variable = ARG_number_of_sens^7
	#clear_variable = ARG_number_of_sens^8
	#clear_variable = ARG_number_of_sens^9
	every_owned_state = {
		limit = {
			has_state_flag = senator_1_cycle_1
		}
		add_to_variable = {ARG.ARG_num_of_sens_cycle_1^ARG_senator_1 = 1}
		add_to_variable = {ARG.ARG_number_of_sens^ARG_senator_1 = 1}
		set_variable = {ARG_senator_2_display = ARG_senator_2}
		add_to_variable = {ARG_senator_2_display = 10}
	}
	every_owned_state = {
		limit = {
			has_state_flag = senator_2_cycle_1
		}
		add_to_variable = {ARG.ARG_num_of_sens_cycle_1^ARG_senator_2 = 1}
		add_to_variable = {ARG.ARG_number_of_sens^ARG_senator_2 = 1}
		set_variable = {ARG_senator_2_display = ARG_senator_2}
		add_to_variable = {ARG_senator_2_display = 10}
	}
	every_owned_state = {
		limit = {
			has_state_flag = senator_1_cycle_2
		}
		add_to_variable = {ARG.ARG_num_of_sens_cycle_2^ARG_senator_1 = 1}
		add_to_variable = {ARG.ARG_number_of_sens^ARG_senator_1 = 1}

		}
		add_to_variable = {ARG.ARG_num_of_sens_cycle_2^ARG_senator_2 = 1}

	clear_variable = ARG_senate_tally
	clear_array = ARG_senate_tally_array
	for_each_loop = {
		array = ARG.ARG_POL_active_parties
		index = idx
		value = party_idx

		set_variable = {ARG_senators^party_idx = ARG_number_of_sens^party_idx}

		add_to_array = {ARG_senate_tally_array = ARG_senate_tally}
		add_to_variable = {ARG_senate_tally = ARG_number_of_sens^party_idx}
	}
	for_each_loop = {
		array = ARG.senate_political_parties
		index = idx
		value = party_idx

		set_variable = {ARG_number_of_senators_display^idx = ARG_senate_tally_array^idx}
		multiply_variable = {ARG_number_of_senators_display^idx = 100}
		add_to_variable = {ARG_number_of_senators_display^idx = ARG_number_of_sens^party_idx}
		multiply_variable = {ARG_number_of_senators_display^idx = 10}
		add_to_variable = {ARG_number_of_senators_display^idx = party_idx}
	}

	ARG_POL_update_amount_of_deps_nationally = yes

	ARG_POL_sortout_senate = yes

	ARG_POL_GUI_update_senate_animation = yes
}

ARG_senate_add_to_locations_array = {

		index = idx

		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					check_variable = {ARG_senator_2_location^party_idx = 0}
				}

ARG_POL_determine_state_leg_split = {
	for_each_loop = {
		array = ARG.ARG_POL_active_parties
		index = idx
		value = party_idx

		set_variable = {total_percent_votes^party_idx = ARG_total_deps_in_state_leg^party_idx}
		divide_variable = {total_percent_votes^party_idx = ARG_state_deputies}
		set_variable = {ARG_POL_percent_of_state_leg^party_idx = total_percent_votes^party_idx}
		multiply_variable = {ARG_POL_percent_of_state_leg^party_idx = 100}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {ARG_state_legislatures > 0}
		}
		for_each_loop = {
			array = ARG.ARG_POL_active_parties
			index = idx
			value = party_idx

			set_variable = {sens_percent_votes^party_idx = ARG_total_sens_in_state_leg^party_idx}
			divide_variable = {sens_percent_votes^party_idx = ARG_state_legislatures}
			add_to_variable = {total_percent_votes^party_idx = sens_percent_votes^party_idx}
			divide_variable = {total_percent_votes^party_idx = 2} #Take an average
			set_variable = {ARG_POL_percent_of_state_leg^party_idx = total_percent_votes^party_idx}
			multiply_variable = {ARG_POL_percent_of_state_leg^party_idx = 100}
		}
	}
	clear_array = ARG_POL_state_leg_percents_for_sorting
	for_each_loop = {
		array = ARG.ARG_POL_active_parties
		index = idx
		value = party_idx

		add_to_array = {ARG_POL_state_leg_percents_for_sorting = ARG_POL_percent_of_state_leg^party_idx}
	}
	clear_array = ARG_sorted_state_leg_control_index
	clear_array = some_fucking_array
	for_each_loop = {
		array = ARG.ARG_POL_active_parties
		index = idx
		value = party_idx

		find_highest_in_array = {array = ARG_POL_state_leg_percents_for_sorting index = kdx}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {ARG_POL_state_leg_percents_for_sorting^kdx > 0}
			}
			set_variable = {ARG_POL_sort_index = kdx}
			add_to_variable = {ARG_POL_sort_index = 1}
			set_variable = {ARG_POL_state_leg_percents_for_sorting^kdx = 0}
			add_to_array = {ARG_sorted_state_leg_control_index = ARG_POL_sort_index}
			add_to_array = {some_fucking_array = ARG_POL_sort_index}
		}
	}
	ARG_GUI_display_pops_in_order = yes
}

ARG_POL_subparties_box_click_effect = {
	set_country_flag = ARG_POL_subpartys_selected
	set_variable = {ARG_POL_coalition = parent_value}
	set_variable = {ARG_POL_which_party_subparty = parent_value:ARG_POL_coalition_members^j}
	every_owned_state = {
		limit = {
			has_state_flag = ARG_election_state
		}
		set_variable = {ARG_POL_subparty = ARG.ARG_POL_which_party_subparty}
		set_variable = {ARG_POL_state_subparty_multiplier = ARG_POL_state_subparties_multiplier^ARG_POL_subparty}
	}
	set_variable = {ARG_POL_tucuman_overlay_frames = 2}
	set_variable = {ARG_POL_caba_overlay_frames = 2}
}
ARG_POL_highlight_all = {
	every_owned_state = {
		limit = {
			has_state_flag = ARG_election_state
		}
		for_loop_effect = {
			start = 0
			end = 192
			value = idx

			set_variable = { ARG_POL_GUI_dep_seat_glow^idx = 1 }
		}
		set_variable = {ARG_POL_GUI_senator_1_highlight = 1}
		set_variable = {ARG_POL_GUI_senator_2_highlight = 1}
		set_variable = {ARG_POL_GUI_state_leg_highlight = 1}
	}
	for_loop_effect = {
		start = 0
		end = 192
		value = idx

		set_variable = { ARG_POL_GUI_dep_seat_glow^idx = 1 }
	}
	for_loop_effect = {
		start = 0
		end = 46
		value = idx

		set_variable = { ARG_senate_highlight^idx = 1 }
	}
}

ARG_POL_clear_election_flags = {
	clr_country_flag = ARG_POL_ongoing_election
	ARG_POL_GUI_clear_highlighted_dots = yes
	clear_variable = ARG_POL_election_year
	clr_country_flag = cycle_1_sen_election
	clr_country_flag = cycle_2_sen_election
	clr_country_flag = cycle_3_sen_election
	clr_country_flag = cycle_1_dep_election
	clr_country_flag = cycle_2_dep_election
	every_owned_state = {
		limit = { has_state_flag = ARG_election_state }
		clr_state_flag = cycle_1_dep_election
		clr_state_flag = cycle_2_dep_election
		clr_state_flag = state_legislature_election
	}
	remove_from_array = {ARG_calendar_boxes = ARG_calendar_boxes^0}
	remove_from_array = {ARG_POL_dep_election_y_position = ARG_POL_dep_election_y_position^0}
	remove_from_array = {ARG_POL_sen_election_y_position = ARG_POL_sen_election_y_position^0}
}
ARG_POL_clear_election_results = {
	for_each_loop = {
		array = ARG.ARG_POL_active_parties
		index = idx
		value = party_idx

		clear_array = party_idx:ARG_national_predicted_deps_change
	}
	#clear_array = 1.PS_national_predicted_deps_change
	#clear_array = 2.UCRP_national_predicted_deps_change
	#clear_array = 3.UCRI_national_predicted_deps_change
	#clear_array = 5.FNPC_national_predicted_deps_change
	#clear_array = 6.NP_national_predicted_deps_change
	#clear_array = 8.PRN_national_predicted_deps_change
	#clear_array = 9.OTHER_national_predicted_deps_change

	every_owned_state = {
		limit = { has_state_flag = ARG_election_state }
		for_each_loop = {
			array = ARG.ARG_POL_active_parties
			index = idx
			value = party_idx

			clear_array = party_idx:ARG_state_predicted_deps_change
			clear_array = party_idx:ARG_state_predicted_sens_change
		}
		#clear_array = 1.PS_state_predicted_deps_change
		#clear_array = 2.UCRP_state_predicted_deps_change
		#clear_array = 3.UCRI_state_predicted_deps_change
		#clear_array = 4.PDC_state_predicted_deps_change
		#clear_array = 5.FNPC_state_predicted_deps_change
		#clear_array = 6.NP_state_predicted_deps_change
		#clear_array = 7.PDP_state_predicted_deps_change
		#clear_array = 8.PRN_state_predicted_deps_change
		#clear_array = 9.OTHER_state_predicted_deps_change
#
		#clear_array = 1.PS_state_predicted_sens_change
		#clear_array = 2.UCRP_state_predicted_sens_change
		#clear_array = 3.UCRI_state_predicted_sens_change
		#clear_array = 4.PDC_state_predicted_sens_change
		#clear_array = 5.FNPC_state_predicted_sens_change
		#clear_array = 6.NP_state_predicted_sens_change
		#clear_array = 7.PDP_state_predicted_sens_change
		#clear_array = 8.PRN_state_predicted_sens_change
		#clear_array = 9.OTHER_state_predicted_sens_change
	}

	for_each_loop = {
		array = ARG.ARG_POL_active_parties
		index = idx
		value = party_idx

		set_variable = {ARG_number_of_sens_predicted_change^party_idx = 0}
	}

	ARG_sort_out_list_of_parties_senate_seats_prediction = yes

	clr_country_flag = presidential_election
}
ARG_update_state_leg_counts = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = ARG_POL_GUI_senate_selected
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {ARG_selected_state:ARG_state_senate_update = 1}
			}
			add_to_variable = {ARG_pol_deps_state_animation_numbers_update = 1}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {ARG_pol_deps_state_animation_numbers_update = 2}
				}
				set_variable = {ARG_pol_deps_state_animation_numbers_update = 0}
				var:ARG_selected_state = {
					ARG_POL_update_state_parliament_animation = yes
				}
			}
			set_variable = {ARG_selected_state:ARG_state_senate_update = 0}
		}
	}
	else = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {ARG_selected_state:ARG_state_congress_update = 1}
			}
			add_to_variable = {ARG_pol_deps_state_animation_numbers_update = 1}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {ARG_pol_deps_state_animation_numbers_update = 2}
				}
				set_variable = {ARG_pol_deps_state_animation_numbers_update = 0}
				var:ARG_selected_state = {
					ARG_POL_update_state_parliament_animation = yes
				}
			}
			set_variable = {ARG_selected_state:ARG_state_congress_update = 0}
		}
	}
}
ARG_update_states_state_leg_animation = {
	#add_to_variable = {ARG_pol_deps_state_animation_update = 1}
	#if = {

	#		check_variable = {ARG_pol_deps_state_animation_update = 2}

				check_variable = {ARG_pol_governor_state_animation_update = 2}
			}
			set_variable = {ARG_pol_governor_state_animation_update = 0}
		}
	}

	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {ARG_selected_state:ARG_state_senators_updated = 0}
		}
		set_variable = {ARG_selected_state:ARG_state_senators_updated = 1}

			limit = {
				check_variable = {ARG_pol_senator_state_animation_update = 2}
			}
			set_variable = {ARG_pol_senator_state_animation_update = 0}
		}
	}
}

ARG_POL_clear_senate = {
	for_loop_effect = {
		start = 0
		end = 46
		value = idx

		set_variable = {ARG_frame_senate_array_display^idx = 10}
	}
	every_owned_state = {
		limit = {
			has_state_flag = ARG_election_state
		}
		for_loop_effect = {
			start = 0
			end = 92
			value = idx

			set_variable = {ARG_POL_GUI_sen_seat_display^idx = 10}
			set_variable = {ARG_POL_GUI_cong_seat_display^idx = 10}
		}
	}
}

	}

	}

ARG_POL_calculate_election_change_state_leg = {
	for_each_loop = {
		array = ARG.ARG_POL_active_subparties
		index = idx
		value = party_idx
